Final Agreement Reached on Inner Mongolian Autonomy 21

Mutual Concessions Between Mongolian Demands and Central Government Proposals

Outline of the Organization of the Autonomous Conference

(Nanjing) Regarding the Inner Mongolian autonomy case, mutual concessions were made between the Mongolian demands and the central government proposals, and a final agreement was reached. The original text: (1) Name: First Autonomous Region Government of Mongolia, Second Autonomous Region Government of Mongolia; (2) Region: Xilingol League and Chahar tribes are compiled as the First Autonomous Region of Mongolia, and Ujimqin League and Alxa Ejin Banner are compiled as the Second Autonomous Region of Mongolia. Other leagues and banners will be compiled into autonomous regions according to this example. (3) Subordination: The autonomous region governments of Mongolia are directly subordinate to the Executive Yuan. In the event of matters involving the provinces, consultations will be held with the provincial governments. (4) Powers: The autonomous region governments of Mongolia manage all political affairs of the leagues and banners within their regions. (5) Funding: The expenses of the autonomous region governments of Mongolia are allocated by the central government on a monthly basis. (6) Liaison: A joint conference will be established between the autonomous regions of Mongolia, organized by one representative elected from each banner within each autonomous region to discuss common matters between the autonomous regions. In addition, the Outline of the Organization of the Autonomous Conference: Article 1: In order to realize Inner Mongolian autonomy, the league and banner leaders of Inner Mongolia convene an Inner Mongolian Autonomy Conference in Bailingmiao. Article 2: Attendees of this conference are the league and banner leaders or their representatives, representatives of Mongolian organizations, and secretaries of the leaders, who may attend the meeting. Article 3: This conference mutually elects five people to form a presidium to preside over all affairs of this conference. Article 4: This conference establishes a secretariat, dividing it into various working groups: document group, agenda group, propaganda group, translation group, finance group, administrative group, communication group, and security group. Article 5: The secretariat has a secretary-general, appointed by the presidium, to manage the affairs of the secretariat. Each group has a director, who, under the order of the secretary-general, presides over the affairs of each group. The secretariat has a number of secretaries, staff members, and clerks, who are divided into various groups to handle affairs. Article 6: The rules of procedure and rules of operation of this conference shall be determined separately. Article 7: This conference shall end when the Inner Mongolian Autonomy Association is realized. Article 8: This outline shall be implemented from the date of its passage by the conference. (Special dispatch from the 24th)

(Nanjing) The representatives of the princes and nobles of various Western Mongolian banners, Senggelinqin and others, came to Nanjing and visited Premier Wang and Chairman Shi of the Mongolian Commission, and on the morning of the 24th, led by Wu Heling, visited the authorities of various military institutions in Nanjing, Zhu Peide, He Yaozu, Dong Musong, etc., to express the sincerity of the princes and nobles of Western Mongolia. (Special dispatch from the 24th)

(Nanjing) Huang Shaoxiong invited the representatives of Inner Mongolia, Zhao Taibao and others, on the morning of the 24th to further discuss the principles of the autonomous region of Mongolia and the organizational law of the regional government. Zhang first stated that the central government has accepted in principle the eleven suggestions signed by the princes and nobles of Inner Mongolia and will submit them to the Central Political Committee for discussion and approval this week, and then the Executive Yuan will formally decide. However, regarding the issue of the autonomous region, such as the old territories of the twelve banners of Chahar, which have already been included in the scope of the Chahar Special Region, are still under the jurisdiction of the Inner Mongolian Autonomous Region Government. The central government is carefully considering this. The organizational law of the regional government must also be approved by the Legislative Yuan to be legal. If the representatives cannot wait for long, then one side will first establish an autonomous preparatory committee, and the other side will be discussed by the Legislative Yuan. The representatives stated: 1. After the Central Political Committee approves the principle of Inner Mongolian autonomy, should the representatives return to Mongolia first, or wait for the preparatory committee of the autonomous region until the ten representatives of the twelve banners of Chahar arrive in Nanjing to discuss and then decide. 2. The biggest issue in this Inner Mongolian request for autonomy is that the old Inner Mongolian territories of the Chahar and Suiyuan special districts must be included in the autonomous region. If the above two districts are still under the jurisdiction of Chahar and Suiyuan, then the scope of Inner Mongolian autonomy will only extend to the barren deserts, which is not the original intention of the representatives' request. 3. Members of the Autonomous Preparatory Committee will be elected by both the Mongolian princes and nobles and the people, but the preparation period will be limited to one month, and the time should not be too long. (Special dispatch from the 24th)

(Nanjing) Minister of Interior Huang Shaoxiong and Deputy Chief of Staff Huang Musong went to the official residence of the Ministry of Railways at Shenshi (3-5 PM) on the 24th to visit Premier Wang to discuss the Inner Mongolian autonomy plan and the Tibetan issue. The discussion lasted for two hours. (Special dispatch from the 2_th)

(Beiping) Huang Shaoxiong previously sent Kong Qingzong, Zheng Qiguang, Yang Junli and others to inspect the Xilingol and Ujimqin leagues of Inner Mongolia. The former has returned to Beiping from Zhangjiakou and drafted an inspection report, which is now complete and will return to Nanjing on the 25th to visit Huang and Shi Qingyang to report on the inspection. (Special dispatch from the 24th)

(Nanjing) The representatives of the princes and nobles of various Mongolian leagues and banners, Ajina Zhana and others, visited Premier Wang and the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission after arriving in Nanjing, expressing their desire for the government to establish a Mongolian autonomous organization as soon as possible. On the 24th, they visited Zhu Peide and reported on the matter. According to reports, representatives of the princes and nobles of various leagues and banners also include Min Guanzhou and others, who are scheduled to depart from Zhangjiakou on the 26th and travel to Nanjing. (Central News Agency telegram from the 24th)

Prince De Appoints Representatives Who Are About to Depart for Nanjing 22

(Beiping) After the Inner Mongolian autonomy issue came to an end, all the leagues and banners sent representatives to Nanjing. However, Prince De has not yet appointed a representative. It is heard that Prince De has appointed three representatives who are scheduled to depart from the Xilingol League at the end of this month and arrive in Beiping on the 4th of next month, and will then transfer to Nanjing to report on everything. Rumors of the Pangjiang Conference are inaccurate. Prince De is currently looking for candidates for representatives and will arrive in Nanjing soon. According to the extent to which Minister Huang verbally agreed in Bailingmiao, the autonomous region government will begin to be established. (Special dispatch from the 24th)

Tibetan Troops Along the Jinsha River Only Have Sentries Deployed 23

Sichuan Troops Have Not Advanced Either

(Nanjing) Liu Wenhui telegraphed that many of the Tibetan troops along the Jinsha River have indeed been transferred back, and only a few sentries are deployed. In order to maintain the Kangding and Ganchazi Peace Agreement, Sichuan troops have not advanced either. (Special dispatch from the 24th)

Tibet Welcomes the Central Government to Send Personnel 24

(Nanjing) The Tibetan Office in Nanjing received a telegram from Tibet stating that they welcome the Central Government's officials to enter Tibet. The office has translated the original telegram and submitted it to the Executive Yuan, the Military Affairs Council, the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, and other relevant agencies. (Special dispatch from the 24th)

The Control Yuan Plans to Advise the Central Government to Reorganize Land Tax as Soon as Possible 25

(Nanjing) The Control Yuan believes that the Central Government has stipulated that the land tax surcharge shall not exceed 59%, and the government has issued an order to all provinces that any increase in surcharges that has not been reviewed by the Legislative Yuan cannot be increased without authorization. However, in recent years, in order to handle security teams and other matters, the surcharges on land tax in various counties have exceeded more than ten times the regular tax, resulting in several lawsuits filed with the Control Yuan by people from various provinces and counties every day. The matter is now being submitted to the Yuan's affairs meeting for discussion, and it has been decided that the members of the Control Committee, Yang Tianji, Yang Lianggong, and others, will review the matter separately and record in detail the exact amount of surcharges in each province. It is planned to advise the Central Government next month to reorganize the land tax as soon as possible in order to relieve the people's hardships. (Special dispatch from the 24th)

Current Affairs Commentary

The Opportunity to Resolve the Kham-Tibet Dispute 28

— Shu

Since the sudden death of the Dalai Lama in Tibet, an opportunity has arisen to resolve the Kham-Tibet dispute. If the central government handles this matter properly this time, the long-standing, crisis-ridden situation in Tibet can be brought to stability, and the western border can gradually become more secure.

The origin of the Tibetan problem lies in Zhao Erfeng's harsh and severe rule over the Tibetan people during the late Qing dynasty. Although the Tibetans were intimidated by military force and dared not revolt immediately, neighboring powers were watching for opportunities, and the local people were contemplating rebellion. After Zhao's departure, the Tibetan border gradually changed. Since the beginning of the Republic, it has implicitly formed a separate political system. However, the Panchen Erdeni, who was stationed in Rear Tibet, was deeply influenced by Tao Rong of the former Qing dynasty. Since the Republic, his inclination towards the interior has never changed, conflicting with the Dalai Lama's pro-British policy. Moreover, the Panchen was focused on his spiritual practice and detached from politics, so the power fell into the hands of the Dalai Lama, and the Panchen had no choice but to travel far to China. Recently, the Dalai Lama seemed to have realized the mistakes of his past pro-British policy and expressed his intention to return to the central government. Therefore, there should be no major problem with the Panchen returning to Tibet after the Dalai Lama's death. However, according to the news reports, the Panchen is still under consideration.

At this time, when the Dalai Lama has passed away and the Panchen has not yet returned, there is a vacuum of power. The Tibetan people mostly follow religious guidance, and the Tibetan region is a region where politics and religion are inseparable. It is natural that people's hearts are unsettled. In addition, India, the treasure house of England, is a neighbor to the south. It has long been making arrangements and clearly harbors the ambition to seize the opportunity for annexation. Only if the Xikang Province, which is adjacent to Tibet, can govern diligently and make the Tibetans feel impressed, and the Han people can secure their livelihoods, no matter how cunning the neighboring powers are, Tibet will not suddenly deviate from the mainland. Now, if we try to examine the internal affairs of Sichuan Province, we can see that under the current situation of separatism, the warlords only know how to defend their own territories and how to plunder their wealth. They have never paid attention to the overall situation in Sichuan, let alone national defense or care about Tibet. Moreover, the troops stationed in the Kangding area lack knowledge and even basic military discipline. They put on airs and show off their power to ordinary Han people, let alone the Tibetan people. Therefore, the resentment between the stationed troops and the local people is growing deeper, and it is difficult for the law to be impartial, so the motivation for rebellion is brewing. Zhao Erfeng's strict measures may have been effective for a time in a unified era. A single brigade may have been enough to govern both Front and Rear Tibet. But now, times have changed. The Tibetans are no longer as easily manipulated as before. In terms of military affairs, they also have modern firearms to fight against the Sichuan army. In terms of knowledge, they have gradually understood politics. The old muddleheaded policies can no longer withstand the gentle deception of others. The central government is far away, and transportation is difficult, so it is beyond its reach. Fortunately, the leader of the pro-British faction is now unable to continue his policies, and the Panchen Lama, who inclines towards the interior, is about to return to Tibet to preside over religious affairs and reorganize the administration. The opportunity to resolve the Kham-Tibet dispute may lie here.

At this time of transition from the old to the new, when the situation is changing, the central government should plan carefully and send senior officials to Tibet to appease the people. In addition to assisting the Panchen's return to Tibet, we should also pay attention to the following points in order to win over the hearts of the Tibetan people and consolidate the national defense of the border region.

First, the key to governing Tibet is to stabilize Sichuan first. Sichuan is Tibet's close neighbor. Although Xikang has been designated as a province, it is still practically a dependency of Sichuan Province. All the negative political influences of Sichuan inevitably affect Xikang, and the corruption of Xikang is easily despised by the Tibetans. Therefore, reorganizing Sichuan is crucial to governing Tibet. Moreover, the people of Sichuan are eager for good governance. As long as the central government has concrete measures and deals with the situation cautiously and resolutely, stabilizing Sichuan will not be difficult.

Second, governing Tibet should involve special policies. Tibet has been influenced by Yellow Buddhism for more than five hundred years, from the Ming dynasty to the present. It has almost become a second nature to them. Its general economic form is also in the early stages of agricultural economy. In addition, it is surrounded by high mountains, and there are few opportunities to absorb knowledge. Now, Inner Mongolia has been granted autonomy. Why can't Tibet also try to implement autonomy suitable to local needs under the guidance of the central government, so that the Tibetan people can have religious freedom and achieve political stability?

Third, pay attention to the diplomacy with the two major neighboring countries to the north and south. Whether it is England or the Soviet Union, both are focusing their attention on Xinjiang and Tibet. Now that the Xinjiang coup has not yet subsided, the Tibetan problem must be re-sorted out. We should renew our diplomatic approach with the neighboring countries that have already set foot in Xinjiang and Tibet. Not only must the borders be clear, but the political relations must also be clearly defined. We must ensure that the northwestern border defense does not repeat the mistakes of the past.

Unprecedented Tragedy on Christmas Eve: Paris Express Trains Collide 32

180 Dead, Over 200 Injured

Holiday Excursion Leads to Unexpected Disaster

Dismembered Limbs and Broken Legs Everywhere

(Paris) - An unprecedented tragedy occurred today in Pomponne near Lagny, France, where an express train between Paris and Strasbourg collided with an express train between Chalons and Troyes. At least 165 people have died, and over 300 are injured. As of 7:00 PM tonight, 165 bodies have been recovered from the wrecked trains, and it is expected that more will be found. At 5:00 PM tonight, the undamaged portion of the Strasbourg express train arrived in Paris, carrying 131 bodies and hundreds of injured. It is reported that almost all passengers on both trains were injured. Even more tragic is that some bodies were still clutching their Christmas food packages. Both trains were full of people on Christmas holiday excursions, and two members of parliament were also among the dead. According to official reports, the accident was caused by the Paris-Strasbourg express train crashing into the rear of the Chalons-Troyes express train. The total number of deaths is estimated to be between 170 and 175. (National News, December 24)

(Paris) - Yesterday evening at 7:00 PM, the special express train between Paris and Strasbourg and the express train between Paris and Nancy collided in Lagny, about 25 kilometers from here. Approximately 180 people were killed and over 200 injured, making it the most tragic train accident of the 20th century. The cause of the accident was the cold weather, ice, dense fog, and poor visibility. The events unfolded as follows: The Paris-Nancy express train, upon reaching about 2 kilometers from the town of Lagny, stopped due to the fog, occupying the track. It lit signals and set off firecrackers to warn oncoming trains. Unfortunately, the Paris-Strasbourg special express train, failing to hear the firecrackers or see the signals, continued at a speed of 100 kilometers per hour and crashed into the last carriage of the express train, smashing it to pieces, and continued forward at the same speed, destroying six passenger carriages in succession. The wreckage was scattered with corpses, a horrifying scene. The sounds of moans never ceased. It was evening, making the scene even more tragic. Rescuers came with lights, moving corpses. Dismembered limbs and broken legs were everywhere. The Paris fire brigade rushed to participate in the rescue. The bishop of Meaux, wearing black mourning clothes, prayed for the dead, tears in his eyes. Premier Chautemps, who was participating in the discussion of the financial bill in the National Assembly until 2:00 AM, heard the news and immediately went to the station with Budget Minister Marchandeau and Minister of Public Works Paganon and took a train to the scene of the accident to investigate and offer condolences. The driver and mechanic of the crashed express train have been arrested and are awaiting trial. Marne Deputy and former Minister of Commerce Roland was severely injured. Also, another train was approaching from the opposite direction at the time of the accident. Fortunately, the driver sensed something unusual and braked urgently, stopping completely 100 meters from the accident site, otherwise the tragedy would have been even more unimaginable. (Havas, December 24)

(Paris) - The baggage room of the Gare de l'Est this morning has been transformed into a morgue, with the corpses arranged outside the iron fence awaiting collection. The first to be prepared for burial was former Minister of Commerce Roland, whose corpse was smashed to pieces, with a gaping hole in his abdomen, a ghastly sight. According to the latest official news, the total number of deaths is 185, including prominent figures such as former Undersecretary Morel, former Minister of Commerce Roland, and Senator Hachette. Premier Chautemps, Chairman of the Paris Municipal Council Fegay, and Police Commissioner Chiappe have all come to pay their respects to the victims. Condolence messages from home and abroad are pouring in. Rescue work is still underway. (Havas, December 24)

Barcelona, Spain - A passenger train departing from here collided with a freight train arriving at the station. A mechanic and a waiter were seriously injured, and over twenty others sustained minor injuries. (Havas, December 24)

US Plans to Implement Bimetallism 38

Adopting New Methods to Raise Prices

Policy of Purchasing Gold Abroad Has Little Effect

Industries Flourishing After England and America Abandon the Gold Standard

(New York) - According to information obtained by the New York Evening Post's Washington correspondent, the US government will soon abandon its policy of buying gold abroad. This policy was originally proposed by Professor Warren, an advisor to President Roosevelt, as a way to raise domestic raw material prices. However, since its implementation two months ago, domestic prices have only risen from 71.5 to 72, with very little effect. Yesterday, the presidents of the Federal Reserve Banks and the members of the Board of Governors held a secret meeting. The result was reportedly to abandon the policy of buying gold. It is also rumored that the government is now planning to adopt new methods to raise prices. According to some sources, President Roosevelt is currently studying a plan that can reconcile the bimetallic system and the theory of "commodity currency." (Havas, December 24)

(Washington) - US House Speaker Rainey stated today that the US government's silver plan may not significantly increase silver prices, but the President's concern for silver is enough to encourage people. He still advocates adopting a bimetallic system, rapidly purchasing silver, and issuing silver certificates that can be exchanged for gold, which would have an effect on restoring 1926 prices that no other plan can achieve. Furthermore, issuing such certificates would eliminate the need to maintain the gold-silver ratio. (National News, December 23)

(Washington) - US Ambassador to England Bingham telegraphed the White House today that industries in both the US and England have seen a surprising recovery since abandoning the gold standard. (National News, December 23)

Hirota Renews Diplomacy and the Foreign Ministry Begins Reorganization 44

Three New Bureaus Established to Adjust Relations with the US, China, and Russia

Developing Trade and Overseas Propaganda Simultaneously Emphasized

(Tokyo) - Foreign Minister Hirota, in order to establish diplomacy in extraordinary times, has begun reorganizing the Foreign Ministry in an attempt to refresh the atmosphere of Japanese foreign affairs. The main points are as follows:

1. Establishment of the Bureau of the Americas: The current Bureau of Europe and America will be divided into two bureaus. In order to adjust diplomatic relations with the countries of North and South America, a new bureau will be established specifically. The Bureau of the Americas will be divided into two sections: The first section will handle political and diplomatic relations, and the second section will protect, supervise, encourage, and handle trade relations with Japanese immigrants in North and South America and with the countries of Central and South America.

2. Establishment of the Bureau of Europe and Asia: Due to the separation of the Bureau of the Americas, the current Bureau of Europe and America will be renamed the Bureau of Europe and Asia, with three sections: The first section will handle diplomatic relations with Soviet Russia and the countries of the Near East. The second section will handle diplomatic issues with Europe, Africa, and the South Pacific. The third section will be a temporary investigation department for arms treaties, investigating and drafting countermeasures for the next disarmament conference.

3. Reorganization of the Bureau of Commerce: The existing organization will be abolished, and the following matters will be handled separately: The first section will handle trade treaty relations, the second section will handle trade affairs relations, and the third section will handle tariff negotiation relations.

4. Reorganization of the Information Department: The current regional division of the Information Department will be abolished, and the following three sections will be established: The first section will handle news and communication propaganda and information affairs. The second section will handle film and broadcasting propaganda and information affairs. The third section will be the same as the current one, handling general affairs.

5. Establishment of the Investigation Department: The Investigation Department will report directly to the Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs and investigate diplomatic negotiations and other cases. The first section will handle the general affairs of the Investigation Department. The second section will coordinate the records and materials of diplomatic negotiations. The third section will investigate relations with Asia and the Near East. The fourth section will investigate relations with Europe and Africa. The fifth section will coordinate diplomatic cases related to North and South America. (Electric Communications Society, December 24)

Japan's Military and Economic Aggression in Manchuria and Mongolia Progresses Simultaneously 45

New Security Organizations Established by the Army and Navy

Decision to Carry Out Economic Aggression

(Changchun) - Since this spring, the Kwantung Army has intensified its aggression in Manchuria, advancing simultaneously along military and economic paths. The main military activities are as follows:

(1) The Naval Department Stationed in Manchuria: The Japanese Navy Ministry established the Naval Department Stationed in Manchuria in Changchun on April 1, with Rear Admiral Hayashi as commander, to guard the coasts and rivers of the puppet state. The puppet state's naval fleet and river defense fleet are under its command.

(2) The Port of Lushun: On April 19, the Navy Ministry also established the Port of Lushun, renovated the Lushun Fortress, and placed the Second Overseas Fleet under the command of its commander, with Rear Admiral Tsuda as its commander.

(3) Establishment of Two New Garrison Units: In order to guard the newly seized Chinese railways and the Russian-Manchurian border, the Japanese Army Ministry appointed Lieutenant Generals Takeda and Sato as commanders, respectively, deciding to station them permanently in Manchuria and Mongolia.

While the Japanese militarists are intensifying their military activities, they have also decided on an economic aggression plan, defining the steps to seize rights and interests. The main activities are as follows:

(1) Unauthorized Reorganization of the Administrative Organization of Jiandao: There are many Japanese-Koreans in the four eastern counties of the Eastern Border Region, accounting for 80% of all Koreans in Manchuria. In March of this year, this region was designated as a special administrative region, and its administrative and police chiefs are uniformly appointed by the Governor-General of Korea.

(2) Self-Defined Commercial Lease Rights Regulations: On February 6, the Kwantung Army self-defined three articles of commercial lease rights regulations, officially announced them, and ordered the county magistrates of the four provinces to follow them.

(3) New Agreement on Japanese-Manchurian Communications: On March 26 of this year, Commander Mutō and the puppet state's foreign minister signed the Japanese-Manchurian Communications Agreement, making all telecommunications and telephone communications businesses under the management of the Japanese.

(4) Self-Defined Outline for Industrial Development: The Kwantung Army self-defined the Outline for Industrial Development of Manchuria and Mongolia and, starting on August 15, held a meeting of Japanese and Manchurian industrialists in Dalian, announcing its policy of monopolizing the industries of Manchuria and Mongolia. 113 representatives from various Japanese business circles attended the meeting, the content of which is omitted.

(5) Establishment of the East Asia Industrial Association: In order to promote Japanese capitalists to go to Manchuria to develop industries, the East Asia Industrial Association was established in Dalian in August of this year. The puppet state bore 500,000 yuan, the South Manchuria Railway Company bore 500,000 yuan, and the Bank of Korea bore 200,000 yuan, totaling 1.2 million yuan. Jitsusami is the chairman, and Zheng Ni is the nominal president. (China United News Agency)

(6) Japan-Manchuria Industrial Association: Japan has also established the Japan-Manchuria Industrial Association in Japan, with Yūki Toyotarō, president of the Industrial Bank of Japan, as chairman. The purpose of this organization is to facilitate investment in Manchuria, mediate disputes between Japanese and Manchurian capitalists, and investigate industrial data in Manchuria and Mongolia.

The Japanese militarists are so actively plotting against us, but still think it is not enough. They plan to reorganize the South Manchuria Railway Company under the control of the militarists and prepare to invade Russia again. This is the main activity of the Japanese militarists in Manchuria in one year. (China United News Agency)

Strange Grass Discovered on Mount Qianfo 81

Its Color Changes Monthly

With Phenomena of Lion and Buddha on Top

Jinan Correspondence: Zhu Dikun, a resident of No. 10 Weixiang Lane, Qian Street, the former provincial government street in Jinan City, stores a grass similar to Lingzhi, which was heard of by the wife of Provincial Chairman Han Fuju. She once asked to take it for a few days to enjoy, and it has now been returned to the original owner. Street talks and alleys discussed it, calling it auspicious, which caused a sensation for a time. According to Zhu's house, the origin of the grass is roughly as follows: Zhu Dikun's eldest son, Xianzhang, is currently 18 years old and is still studying. After the Mid-Autumn Festival, Zhu Xianzhang and three or four classmates went to Mount Qianfo south of the city to visit. They strolled through the peaks and reached the west side of the mountain, where there was a thousand-foot-high cliff, with an ancient cypress tree below, which could be counted in circles, reaching five feet in height. The branches and trunks reached the sky, and it was a century-old object. Zhu looked far away and occasionally saw a colorful butterfly. He rushed forward to catch it, touched it, and it turned into a strange grass, of unknown name. Because of its strangeness, he took it home and carefully studied it. Its texture is as hard as stone, but it is extremely light. Other kinds of grass can pass through its head and be attached to it to grow. The next day, Zhu's family members went to the original discovery site with hoes to search for its roots, but they found only mixed soil and stones and nothing else. After the news spread, the threshold of those who went to see it every day was almost broken. Some people said that the Lingzhi recorded in the Flora was quite similar to this. As for the shape of the grass, it is roughly the same as a mushroom, but its texture is not a mushroom. It is about four inches high, with a stem, shaped like an old man's neck, with wrinkles and spots, and like a dead tree. The top gradually widens, shaped like a fan, and spreads forward. There is a white membrane underneath, which gradually shrinks, with fragrant grass and Hushan green grass passing through it. There are only whisker marks. It is as light as nothing when held, and makes a clang when knocked, like striking a stone chime. Soft green grass can be pierced through it. The color is black and red, close to deep purple. According to Zhu Dikun, its color changes monthly, from red to purple, and then from purple to red, endlessly circulating. It is suspected to be meat Ganoderma, a discovery that has not occurred for thousands of years. If you look at it with a magnifying glass, there are phenomena such as lions and Buddhas on it. It is indeed a strange thing. (22nd)

Page 7

After the Japanese Government's Budget for the Next Fiscal Year is Finalized (Tokyo, Japan) 82

The Crisis Has Not Diminished

Political Upheaval is Still Brewing

The Military is Highly Alert

Public Dissatisfaction is High

Since the military proposed a state of emergency, which has enveloped the entire country of Japan, parliamentary politics have been paralyzed, and the military has indeed made progress. The arrogance of the military has forced those engaged in political work to become mere tools of the military. However, we know that the Saitō Cabinet was originally intended to be a cabinet to weather the so-called state of emergency. Therefore, the composition of the cabinet included many representatives of capital conglomerates. Even if cabinet members from political parties lean towards the military, they are by no means willing to easily abandon the interests of capitalists. As a result, financial problems arose because the budget was excessively expanded.

Among these problems, the first is the opposition between the Army and the Ministry of Finance, and the second is the opposition between the Navy and the Ministry of Finance. To put it bluntly, it is the opposition between the military and financial cliques. Under normal circumstances, since the Saitō Cabinet contained such huge contradictions, the cabinet would inevitably collapse, or the military would emerge to lead the formation of a cabinet, or the financial clique would rise up to become a financial oligarchy. However, none of these things actually happened because the military did not dare to risk causing domestic unrest, and the financial clique did not have the strength to suppress the military. Therefore, they finally managed to find a temporary way to ease the situation. The budget proposed by the Army has indeed been greatly reduced, and the Navy's so-called second supplementary plan, the renovation of battleships, and the establishment of air wings are said to be indispensable. The Saitō Cabinet was almost unable to maintain itself because of this, but in the end, it was still a compromise. At the beginning of this month, the number of expenditures for the next fiscal year decided by the cabinet was 2.11 billion yen, a decrease of over 128 million yen compared to this year's 2.239 billion yen. Then, isn't the so-called budget expansion incorrect? It is not known that there is a reason for this, which is that the new special accounting will be separated independently from next year. The special accounting belonging to the communication industry has 190 million yen, which is calculated separately. If this amount is added to the budget, the budget for the next fiscal year will be 62 million yen more than this year. The total amount of expenditures will be 2.3 billion yen, an unprecedentedly huge figure.

If we compare it with the situation three years ago, the expenditure budget in 1931 was only 1.488 billion yen. In these three years, it has jumped by 800 million yen, what a huge change in finance! Let's take a look at the newly increased content in terms of expenditures. The total of regular expenses and temporary expenses is 723 million yen. Among this huge increase, the increased interest on public bonds and the repayment of foreign debts, and the losses due to the depreciation of the Japanese yen exchange rate, must spend 110 million yen. The so-called current affairs assistance expenses, combined with the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, are only 52 million, and the remaining more than 560 million yen are mostly used for military purposes. The Army's new request to increase the number is 248 million yen, the Navy's is 234 million, and the total of the Army and Navy is 483 million yen. The total of the remaining new requests is only over 78 million yen. This is the performance of Japan's so-called national defense.

If we add up the regular expenses and temporary expenses in the military, the Army's military expenditure is 448 million, the Navy's military expenditure is 488 million, and the total military expenditure of the Army and Navy is 936 million, accounting for more than 44% of the total expenditure. This is really an alarming military expenditure in a state of emergency. Who can say that Japan is not actively preparing for war?

So ignorant, it is not surprising that the general public in Japan often have dissatisfied discussions in the streets and corners. Therefore, dangerous ideas are constantly developing. There is a gradually universal resistance movement against such blind military adventurism, and there are also many dissenting voices from the capitalist side. Therefore, on the 9th of this month, the Army and Navy specifically issued a statement in the form of a conversation, saying that there is a crisis in 1936, saying that the military does not sacrifice the interests of the common people, and saying that national defense should be and is necessary. But what is the effect? It is not yet visible. From a fair observation, it is also thought that it is equal to the theory of the divine country, which does not help the panic of the Japanese people. (December 19th in Tokyo)

National Army Recaptures Chong'an 83

The Central Army of Jiangxi, Fujian, and Zhejiang Completes Liaison

Nanchang Correspondence: After the Northern Route Army recaptured Guangze, it has established close contact with the troops of Liu Heding, Zhou Zhiqun, and Zhang Luanji in northern Fujian. Zhang's brigade arrived in Chong'an on the 20th and fought fiercely with more than 2,000 bandits for a day and night, killing many bandits. On the 21st, Chong'an City was recovered. Chong'an borders Zixi, Guixi, Qianshan, and Shangrao in eastern Jiangxi to the west, Shaowu and Jianyang to the south, Pucheng and Songxi to the north, and is also connected to Zhenghe and Jian'ou. It is extremely important to the military affairs of the borders of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Fujian. However, the central army in Shaowu, Guangze, Chong'an, Pucheng, and Songxi in northern Fujian has large armies arriving, and large armies are also gathering along the above-mentioned areas of eastern Jiangxi, western Zhejiang, and southern Zhejiang. It is expected that the Fujian army and the Jiangxi bandits will not succeed. (December 22nd)

Resolution of the Yufeng Cotton Mill Dispute 84

The labor-management dispute at the Zheng County Yufeng Cotton Mill was resolved on the 20th of this month. The mediation decision and the maintenance fee settlement method are recorded below:

▲Mediation Decision (1) With the consent of both labor and management, the mediation decision made by labor and management on August 16 of this year, as amended this time, is incorporated into this decision. All previous contracts established between labor and management shall be invalid from the date of signing this decision. (2) Except as provided in this decision, both labor and management shall abide by the Factory Law, Trade Union Law, and their implementing regulations. No additional complications shall arise, and all disputes shall be permanently resolved. (3) In accordance with Article 10 of the Factory Law, the working hours of each shift are extended to twelve hours. Each worker shall be paid according to their actual working hours. Those who do not complete the stipulated working hours for each shift shall be settled proportionally. (4) The factory shall resume full operation on January 5, 1934, employing 3,582 workers. Based on this number of workers (i.e., 3,582), the total wages for both day and night shifts are set at 1,733 yuan, including bonuses, night meal allowances, and overtime pay (detailed wage schedules to be compiled by the factory). According to the following clauses, the factory may reduce the number of workers and the total daily wages: (A) The factory may, at its discretion, not replace workers who die or resign. If workers are not replaced, the total daily wage of 1,733 yuan shall be reduced accordingly. (B) In order to determine the number of surplus workers in the factory, a committee of seven members shall be established, with three members appointed by the Director of the Henan Construction Department, three members appointed by the Chairman of the China Cotton Control Commission, and one manager of the Yufeng Cotton Mill. They shall conduct a joint investigation and submit three copies of their report by June 15, 1934, one to the Director of the Henan Construction Department, one to the factory manager, and one to the labor union. Both parties shall accept the majority's decision as stated in the report, and there shall be no changes during the validity period of this decision. The factory may dismiss the remaining surplus workers under this decision by June 30, 1934, and revise the daily wage schedule for the remaining workers on July 1 of the same year. One-third of the daily wages saved by dismissing the surplus workers shall be added to the wages of the remaining workers. The dismissed surplus workers shall each be paid wages for the notice period stipulated in Article 5 of this decision. (5) In the future, when the factory reduces workers, it shall pay wages for the following stipulated notice periods, and no other expenses shall be paid: (A) For those who have worked continuously in the factory for three months or more but less than one year, a ten-day notice shall be given. (B) For those who have worked continuously in the factory for one year or more but less than three years, a twenty-day notice shall be given. (C) For those who have worked continuously in the factory for three years or more, a thirty-day notice shall be given. (6) From January 5, 1934, the practice of paying maintenance fees or other allowances during the factory's shutdown period shall be abolished and replaced by the following provisions. In the future, if the factory shuts down again, workers working in the factory shall be paid the following maintenance fees during the continued shutdown period: (A) No maintenance fee shall be paid from the date of shutdown to the 15th day. (B) From the 16th day to the 30th day, each person shall be paid a total maintenance fee of two yuan. (C) From the 31st day onwards, each person shall be paid a maintenance fee of one jiao per day. (7) Bonuses and night meal allowances (both specified in Article 4), school expenses, bathhouse expenses, hospital medication provisions, death condolences, and memorial days shall be paid as before. However, those who are absent from work shall have their wages deducted as before. This method shall be implemented according to the old practice before the shutdown on July 29 of this year. Female workers shall enjoy the benefits stipulated in Article 37 of the Factory Law. (8) In accordance with Article 40 of the Factory Law, the factory shall allocate two-fifteenths of the net profit at the end of each year to be distributed to the workers as bonuses. (9) When the factory hires workers, it shall give due consideration to workers recommended by the labor union, but the factory shall have the freedom to hire or reject them and may hire workers not recommended by the labor union. (10) This decision shall be effective from the date of signing to December 31, 1936, and both parties shall abide by it. Signed on December 20, 1933, by labor representatives Wang Zili and Niu Songxing, factory representative Dong Chusheng, Garrison Headquarters representative Li Jilie, Construction Department Director Zhang Jingyu, First District Administrative Commissioner Ruan Fanqi, County Party Affairs Officer Lu Yan, Chamber of Commerce President Zhang Boqin, Public Security Bureau Director Xu Feiyou, and Local Court representatives Xiao Yuncheng and Han Qingwen.

▲Maintenance Fee Settlement Method There are disputes among all parties regarding the interpretation of the contract provisions signed by labor and management on August 16 of this year for maintaining the workers during this shutdown. Both parties are now willing to resolve the matter as soon as possible and handle it with a friendly attitude. (1) All workers who were working in the factory before July 29 of this year (regardless of any demands, all have been completely resolved) shall be paid as follows: (A) Retained workers shall receive maintenance fees from July 29 of this year to January 4, 1934. (B) The 555 dismissed workers shall receive maintenance fees from July 29 of this year to January 28, 1934. (2) The factory shall pay the remaining amount owed to the workers as stated in Article 1 within seven days after the signing of this contract. Signed on December 20, 1933. (Signatories as above)

Local Products Along the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Road 85

Exhibition of Local Products to be Held

on the Day of the Opening Ceremony

The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Road starts from Xixing on the right bank of the Qiantang River in Hangzhou, passes through Xiaoshan, Zhuji, Yiwu, Jinhua, Tangxi, Longyou, Qu County, Jiangshan, and reaches Yushan in Jiangxi. All the areas along the route are rich in local products. Now that the entire line has regular bus service, it is convenient for the export of local products from various counties along the line. The timber, bamboo, winter bamboo shoots, dried bamboo shoots, tea, and medicinal materials from the old Longquan, Songyang, and Suichang areas, as well as the porcelain, summer cloth, white paper, tea, tobacco, and coal from eastern Jiangxi, can also be promoted and sold. The Construction Department will hold a local product exhibition along the line when holding the opening ceremony on the 28th, to show the richness of eastern Zhejiang's local products, which urgently need to be sold abroad. The reporter has made a special investigation of the local products along the road as follows, so that readers who are unable to attend the exhibition can also learn about them.

Salt 86

Zhejiang Province produces salt in various coastal areas, with Yuyao and Shaoxing counties as the center. Yuyao produces 180,000 yin of sun-dried salt annually (each yin is 370 market catties), which is sold throughout the 26 counties in the Zhejiang salt area, with each yin worth 4 to 6 yuan, and a total value of 800,000 to 900,000 yuan. It produces 20,000 yin of boiled salt, with a total value of more than 100,000 yuan. The Shaoxing salt sales area is the old Jinquyan area and 22 counties including Tonglu and Fuyang, as well as Guangxin in Jiangxi and the three counties of Yixiu and Shexian in southern Anhui. Among them, Guangxin County has the largest sales volume, reaching more than 30,000 yin annually, Xiuning about 20,000 yin, and Jiangshan, Kaihua, Lanxi, and Zhuji each about 12,000 to 13,000 yin. The total annual sales are more than 200,000 yin. The brine crystals from the Yuyao and Shaoxing salt farms have a total annual value of 6,000 to 7,000 yuan.

Rice and Tea 87

Xiaoshan, Zhuji, Yiwu, Wuyi, Yongkang, Jinhua, Lanxi, Longyou, and Qu County all produce rice, with Jinhua, Longyou, and Qu County being the most abundant. The annual output is about 1.2 million dan in Jinhua, about 100,000 dan in Longyou, and about 300,000 dan in Qu County, totaling 1.6 million dan, valued at 13.6 million yuan. The tea-producing areas along the line are most abundant in Zhuji, Pujiang, Dongyang, Wuyi, Xianju, Changshan, Kaihua, Jiangshan, Yushan, and Wuyuan, with an annual output of more than 40,000 dan, valued at 1.5 to 1.6 million yuan.

Livestock 88

Livestock is a sideline of farmers. Among them, cattle are raised in the largest numbers in Zhuji, Xianju, Lanxi, Qu County, Yiwu, and Yongkang. The annual output is about 33,000 heads, with a total value of more than 1.97 million yuan. Farmers raise pigs most commonly in the old Jingshu Dongyang, Jinhua, Yongkang, Yiwu, Wuyi Lanxi, Pujiang, Qu County, and Longyou. Farmers take pig manure to fertilize the soil, and feed them with barley and miscellaneous grains, so the meat is tender and delicious, far better than the pigs in northern Jiangsu. Jinhua and Quzhou can produce more than 900,000 pigs annually. In addition to being used for making ham, more than 173,000 pigs can be exported, with a total value of more than 3.3 million yuan.

Ham 89

The old Jingshu Dongyang, Lanxi, Yiwu, Pujiang, and Yongkang all produce ham, with Dongyang being the most abundant. The annual output is about 6,000 pieces, each made with 40 to 50 pigs, valued at 120 to 150 yuan, with a total value of about 800,000 yuan, mostly sold in Hangzhou. Lanxi is the second largest, mostly sold in Shanghai. Yiwu, Yongkang, and Pujiang each account for half of Dongyang's output. Jinhua produces about 1,000 pieces annually. Tangxi and Wuyi export very little. The forelegs of pigs are pickled into wind meat. The output is the largest in Yiwu, Pujiang, and Dongyang counties, with an annual output of about 5,000 pieces, valued at 250,000 yuan.

Paper 90

Qu County and Longyou are famous for producing paper. The paper produced in Longyou is mostly Nanping paper, which is sold in Shanghai, Hangzhou, Changzhou, and various parts of Shandong, Henan, and Hebei, with an annual output of about 135,000 pieces. The second is fancy paper, about 15,000 pieces, all used for sacrifices. The next is yellow paper, also used for superstitions. The total of Nanping and fancy paper is 150,000 pieces, valued at 900,000 yuan. Qu County paper also has three types: Nanping, fancy paper, and yellow paper. The annual output of the three items is 300,000 dan, valued at 2.2 to 2.3 million yuan. In addition, Lianshi Guan Sanjian paper is produced in Shuitang and other places near Yushan.

Summer Cloth 91

Summer cloth is produced in Yushan, Shangrao, Fuzhou, and Wanzai. Previously, Yushan exported 16,000 tubes (12 pieces per tube), but now only 5,000 tubes. Shangrao exported 10,000 tubes, but now only 4,000 tubes. The products of Yushan and Shangrao are both coarse summer cloth, used for making mosquito nets. Wanzai used to produce about 5,000 tubes, which was fine summer cloth. Tongxing and Linchuan products were famous at the time, but now there is no output.

Porcelain 92

Longquan has a long history of producing porcelain. The products of Ge Kiln and Di Kiln in Nanxiang were famous in the Song Dynasty, and their products were treasured at home and abroad. In recent years, due to poor management, the annual output is only 20,000 to 30,000 yuan. Zhuji has sand kilns that burn sand jars and wine altars, with total annual sales of more than 300,000 yuan. The porcelain of Jingdezhen could originally be transported to Yushan via Raozhou Huangjinbu and Hekou, with annual sales of 200,000 to 300,000 dan, but recently there have been frequent banditry, and many porcelain kilns have been destroyed.

Talc 93

There are many talc mines along the line. There are 26 talc mining areas in Pujiang, Yiwu, Jinhua, Tangxi, Suichang, Longyou, Jiangshan, Changshan, etc., with reserves of 644,373 metric tons. When mining began in 1917, the annual output was about 400 tons. There was a period of stagnation in 1919 and 1920. From 1921 to 1925, the total output was 11,000 tons. From 1926 to 1930, the annual average was about 8,000 tons, with 1928 being the most prosperous, with an output of more than 11,000 tons. After the January 28 Incident, sales declined sharply, and many stopped mining. It is said that 90% of the talc in Zhejiang Province is sold to the Japanese.

Tung Oil 94

Tung trees and cypress trees are planted everywhere on the hillsides and fields of Zhuji, Pujiang, Yiwu, Dongyang, Jinhua, Yongkang, Lanxi, Shouchang, Jiande, Qu County, Changshan, and Jiangshan. The oil industry is particularly prosperous. After tung oil was exported to the United States, sales increased, making it a major export product of our country today. Cypress oil is also exported to the United States to make stearic acid candles and Stearin. In 1932, the output of tung oil along the line was more than 166,400 dan, valued at more than 2.94 million yuan. In 1932, the output of cypress oil was about 113,214 dan, valued at more than 1.89 million yuan.

Other products, such as sugarcane in Tangxi, Longyou, and Qu County, oranges in Qu County, and fir wood and charcoal in Longquan, Songyang, and Suichang, are also produced in large quantities, but are omitted here.

Inspection Notes on Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan, and Hubei by Ren An, Special Correspondent of This Newspaper 95

Miscellaneous News After the Robbery in Southern Henan (Continued)

I got off the train at Xinyang. At six o'clock the next morning, I transferred to a bus and went east, passing through Luoshan. At three o'clock in the afternoon, I arrived at Huangchuan. I was inspected upon entering the city. Even my lined clothes and cotton quilt had to be felt one by one. The inspection of the entire train compartment took more than an hour. The intention was probably to focus on drugs. A river divides the city into two, with a long bridge connecting them. The people in the streets of the city were usually deserted. At that time, the banknotes issued by a certain army suddenly lost their credit, and the city's finances were extremely chaotic. There were quite a few shops that announced they were settling accounts and suspending business. Soldiers accounted for the majority of those coming and going in the market. Women were rarely seen. Occasionally, a few women would slowly enter and exit the shops, and they would always be followed by several armed soldiers, which attracted crowds of villagers to watch. Women rarely go out. Is this due to the customs of the north, or is it due to the special circumstances at the time? It is a pity that I could not find out. The so-called special goods are sold exclusively by a certain public store designated by the Hubei Special Goods Resident Henan Commissioner's Office. If anyone sells or buys privately without affixing special tax labels, once caught, in addition to being dealt with in accordance with the anti-smoking regulations, the offender's assets will also be confiscated. It is also said that someone was caught privately selling heroin (it is said that it is still opium paste and not real heroin) and has been shot. These were all learned from the newly posted notices on the wall.

Regarding the construction of the Huangchuan New Village, I went to the headquarters to inquire, but I did not get any clues. I was transferred to the county government, and I learned that the so-called New Village plan was proposed by Hu Shiqing, a shareholder of the Henan Zhongyuan Company. Although the authorities intended to adopt it, it has not yet been implemented. The rumor that there is a New Village Office in Huangchuan is also completely false. In terms of the immigration policy, Commander Liu estimates that the funding required is more than 4 million yuan, but only 100,000 yuan has been received, so it is impossible to start. I traveled thousands of miles to come here, and suddenly I heard this statement, and a burst of joy turned into a cold-hearted ice heart. The Chinese people have always liked to exaggerate and boast, often using blank paper and empty words to show off. The situation this time is exactly like this. The reporter was unwilling to make this trip in vain, so he specially asked the county government to issue a passport and changed it to an inspection of the "Jingfu" County, which was established in the recovered area. The information obtained is recorded as follows:

Jingfu County was originally the Xinjizhen Township of Guangshan. It was lost for more than two years. In the autumn of last year, it was recovered by Tang Shi, part of General Liu Zhi's army in Henan. Commander-in-Chief Chiang, based on the needs of the terrain, rebuilt the county seat, so it was named Jingfu after Liu's name, and the county was named after it. The area is surrounded by mountains on all sides, with Guangshan and Luoshan to the north, Shangcheng and Lihuang (formerly a famous Red area Jinzhai, recovered by Wei Lihuang's army, was renamed the county after Wei's name) to the east, and Macheng and Huang'an to the south, all hundreds of miles away. There is a solid stone city, mostly inhabited by gentry and landlords, which has long been coveted by the Red bandits, and they wanted to seize the land in order to connect with the Red Army in Shangcheng and Huang'an, as a base for spying on Wuhan. On the 7th of July in 1919, the Red Fourth Army and the Twenty-fifth Army troops launched a large-scale siege. They did not take it down for more than a month. The bandits then tunneled and bombed the north city. With a loud noise, dust rose high, and the city wall collapsed by dozens of feet. The civil defense team in the city paid full attention to this. Unexpectedly, the bandits adopted the method of making a feint in the east and attacking in the west. On one side, they climbed the city wall from the south and entered the entire city. In order to prevent the defense from being solid, all the city gates were filled with wood, stones, and cloth bags, and it was impossible to escape in a hurry. Everyone was afraid and laid down in the city, and no one was safe. Later, in order to implement their doctrine and suppress counter-revolutionaries, those who were generally regarded as local tyrants and evil gentry were arrested, killed, and punished as easily as taking something out of a pocket. The disaster was more severe than elsewhere. The reason is here.

The bandits first attacked the city several times, large and small, for more than a year. The city was firmly defended and they failed to succeed. This time, it was captured because they were afraid that it would be difficult to occupy it for a long time, so they demolished the city walls in advance in order to recapture it in the future. And they judged the situation and established the Soviet Government of the Hubei, Henan, and Anhui Border Region here. The first step was to confiscate the fields of officials, tyrants, and gentry, and other land. The village was the unit, and the land was distributed according to the population and labor of middle peasants, poor peasants, and hired peasants. A mass meeting of the whole village was convened, and land commissioners were elected from the workers and peasants. The Land Committee was organized by 17 to 21 people. The gong was sounded to gather the people, and they went to step on the fields and mountains together. First, the Red Army's public land was taken out and divided, and then the nearby and distant fields, mountains, forests, ponds, and bamboo gardens were calculated as a total. The good and bad were matched and mixed for division. The list of divided land was posted. If someone thought that the division was not good, they could propose revisions. The Workers and Peasants Supervision Committee, the Red Party's various levels of supervision committees, and the Political Department of the Bandit Army all accepted lawsuits for unfair land distribution. The general workers, hired peasants, poor peasants, and especially the family members of the bandit army, were able to raise their heads greatly and actively attack the rich peasants and landlords. The disaster of killing was also very tragic.

At the same time, they also forced the formation of teams according to gender and age. Those from eight to fourteen years old were the Young Pioneers, those from fifteen to twenty were the Youth Vanguard, those from twenty-one to forty were the Red Guards, guerrillas, transportation teams, and stretcher teams. There was also an obligation to join the Red Army. The young and strong of the women were organized into comfort teams, and the middle-aged were organized into laundry or sewing teams. There were also production teams, and men, women, and children were required to participate as much as possible, mobilizing manpower and animal power to help those who lacked manpower and animal power in other places to cultivate. If there was wasteland to be reclaimed, criminals with lighter crimes were organized into reclamation teams to work hard. The suffering of the people cannot be described in a word.

The area is mountainous and dangerous, bordering three provinces. The successive attacks by the National Army were not uniformly commanded, and the situation was different, making it difficult to make progress. The bandit area was expanded, and there was a tendency to flee east to Bengbu. Later, the General Headquarters for Diligence in Suppressing Bandits in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui was established. Commander-in-Chief Chiang came to Wuhan to supervise the suppression, and Deputy Commander Li Jishen was stationed in Bengbu to provide support. Liu Zhi, the director of appeasement in Henan, also came to Luoshan to supervise the army. The various forces advanced together and successively recovered various places. The bandit forces became increasingly isolated. Liu's army, led by Tang, advanced towards Xinjizhen, beheading hundreds of bandits, and finally recovered the city. Jingfu County was newly established, and city walls and bunkers were built, and the Baojia system was established. Although there are still a small number of gray civilians and sporadic bandits who are stubbornly resisting in remote areas, and are thinking of moving. Now that Liu Zhenhua, the commander of the Bandit Suppression Headquarters in the border area of the three provinces, is stationed in Huangchuan, suppressing and appeasing at the same time, the area has been pacified. The Red bandit military supplies seized include a Ningsi No. 4 aircraft, more than ten mortars and pistols, more than twenty machine guns, three or four thousand rifles, and countless items from the pseudo-cooperative and various levels of Soviet government. It is said that there is still a part of the scattered bandits hiding sharp weapons in the deep mountains and forests, who are like desperate bandits. They go down the mountain in the middle of the night and assassinate those who have surrendered and reformed, calling it "touching the melon." Their whereabouts are uncertain. It is feared that there will be changes if they are recruited, and there is no way to capture them if they are killed. They are now being collected by the civilians and strong men in the mountains, hoping to eliminate their traces and secure the four borders.

Business in the city is deserted, and refugees are gathered, suffering from cold and hunger, and there are many sick people. The scene is bleak and unbearable to see. Most of the goods sold are cigarettes, alcohol, food, and paper. Most of the buyers are military and political personnel. Villagers rarely enter the city unless they are selling firewood or buying salt. There is only one newly established elementary school in the entire territory, with more than thirty students. The funds are only the county government's monthly subsidy of 20 yuan, and the county government's political expenses are maintained by the provincial government, which is also very limited. The opinions of the local people, military and political circles on the aftermath measures vary, and their opinions differ. Some say that it is appropriate to start with solving the land problem, thinking that the banditization of the people is not their original intention. It is actually due to the opposition between the tenants and the landlords, the disparity between the rich and the poor, and the instigation of the Red Party, which led to taking risks. If they can be properly appeased and made to cultivate the land with peace of mind, they will be influenced and abide by the law. Some say that it is appropriate to handle the immigration policy, thinking that the people in the bandit area have been deeply banditized. If the environment and air are not changed, it is difficult to guarantee that they will not repeat their old tricks if they encounter special objective conditions. Therefore, they advocate moving out the people who have been banditized and leading good people from other places to move in and cultivate the land. The former has no proper rules and regulations to follow, and the latter is working hard to try it out, but unfortunately it is limited by funding and has not yet seen any results.

Songjiang

Dispute Among Fishmongers Causes Trouble 96

Caojing is located on the coast of this county, and the residents all live by fishing and salt. The other day, a fisherman went out to sea to fish and returned fully loaded. He sold it to Jiang Zhengxing Fish Firm. Unexpectedly, Jiang Zhaoji Fish Firm solicited at a high price. The two fish firms quarreled with each other, and Jiang Zhaoji Fish Firm actually held this resentment and lured the brothers of Jiang Zhengxing Fish Firm to the coast. Taking them by surprise, they pushed them into the sea. At that time, the tide was rolling in. The brothers of Jiang Zhengxing Fish Firm drank their fill of salt water. Although they were rescued by people in time, their throats were damaged and they have not yet recovered. The victimized brothers of Jiang Zhengxing Fish Firm will file a negotiation with the owner of Jiang Zhaoji Fish Firm.

Female Corpse Found Floating in Xin Zhuang 97

A female corpse was found floating in the Dahebang River in Yangqi, outside of the Xin Zhuang train station. Her hair was gray, and she was wearing a blue cotton-padded jacket and pants. Her face was blurred. The patrol leader Zhang Jiasheng of the branch station discovered it and went to check it with the village police Zhou Fangxian. He tied the corpse and had Zhou guard it. Patrol leader Zhang reported back to the county public security bureau and sent a letter to the county court for inspection. The cause of the death has not yet been determined.

Wuxi

Passenger Dies After Jumping From Train 98

The twelfth train bound for Beijing from Shanghai passed through Shuitangwan Station in this county and entered Yangqi, outside of the east gate, at about 2 p.m. yesterday. A man of about forty years of age, wearing mourning clothes, suddenly jumped down and fell to the ground. His head was broken and bleeding. By the time he was picked up, his face was blurred, and he was seriously injured and unable to speak. Before long, he died. The Tu Zheng of that place reported to this county's court, and the appointed prosecutor led the officials to inspect the body. It was confirmed that he had died from injuries sustained in the fall. Because no family members could be found, the Tu Zheng was ordered to collect the body and put it in a coffin.

Jointly Organize Civilian Factory 99

Tianxu Wo Sheng Chen Diexian, the owner of the Shanghai Family Industry Society, Li Yinbei, the resident representative of the China United Society in Wuxi, and Chen Rongxuan, the director of the Lizhi Paper Mill, and Wu Bangzhou, the director of the Civilian Training Center, recently jointly initiated the organization of a civilian factory in order to implement the self-made and self-sufficient method of production and sales, to reduce the burden on consumers and increase the strength of producers. The total capital was set at 20,000 yuan, which will be fully subscribed by the initiators. The draft contract for the initiation method has been drawn up by Tianxu Wo Sheng and was sent to Wuxi yesterday. After the review by Li and the Lizhi Paper Mill Civilian Training Center, a founding meeting will be held on a scheduled date. The official opening date will be in mid-January next year.

Changzhou

Police Team Arrests Armed Bandit 100

Yao Liangxiao, a notorious bandit who has repeatedly committed crimes at the border of Wujin and Danyang, is feared by the surrounding people. Yin Xicai, the patrol leader of the Fifth Squad directly under the Wuyi Police Team, recently received a tip that the bandit was passing by a certain place and going to Xinqiao in Danyang. He immediately led several police officers to rush to catch him. He captured Yao Liangxiao and found a pistol in his sister's house. He also searched everywhere for accomplices and successively captured suspected bandits Yao Wanshu, Wang Fuxing, Zhang Si, Yang Jiu, Wu Xiaosanzi, Tao Honggen, Cai Zhaosheng, Cai Yaoshi, and others. Yao Liangxiao's confession was firm and he did not reveal the truth. After repeated strict questioning, he confessed that he had robbed Chen Hongfan's house outside the north gate of Mengcheng. Yao Wanshu and Wang Fuxing, who came with him this time, were prepared to commit crimes together. Patrol leader Yin immediately transferred the witnesses to the police team headquarters. The team leader Mao Gangsheng transferred all the witnesses to the county government for interrogation yesterday (23rd).

Zhenjiang

New Weights and Measures Must Be Used for Medicine 101

Since the Zhenjiang County Government promoted the new weights and measures system, all industries in the provincial capital area have gradually become uniform. However, the medical and pharmaceutical industries have not yet complied with the changes, which is quite inappropriate. It is now planned to formally announce the completion of uniformity on January 1, 1934, with no further delays. Previously, an order from the Construction Department was issued to various counties in Jiangsu Province regarding the implementation of weights and measures for Chinese medicine, along with a conversion table between the old and new systems. This has been completed, submitted, and approved. To ensure cautious implementation and to facilitate the simultaneous implementation of both Chinese medicine and pharmaceutical industries, one copy each of the implementation methods for weights and measures for Chinese medicine in Jiangsu Province and the conversion table between the old and new systems for weights and measures for Chinese medicine in Zhenjiang County have been printed and distributed for application in both industries. It is stipulated that the new system will be implemented simultaneously starting from January 15th. All medical prescriptions must have a stamp indicating "Changed to New System" on the upper right corner, with a signature or seal and the date filled in the lower left corner to clarify responsibility. Yesterday, the methods and conversion tables were announced to all residents of the county for their general knowledge.

Yangzhou

High School Girl Flees in Shame and Indignation 102

Zhang Yanglan, an 18-year-old first-year student at Jiangdu County Junior High School, is the daughter of Zhang Futong, an accountant at the Yangzhou Audit Branch. She received elementary education at home from a young age. This year, she took the entrance examination twice and was admitted to the school. During the exams a month ago, she failed two subjects, causing her great distress. Later, she heard the principal encourage students, stating that those who fail two subjects in the second monthly exam will be expelled. Upon hearing this, the student felt even more ashamed and indignant and doubled her efforts. However, she still failed two subjects in the second monthly exam. The student, feeling she was not making progress in her studies, developed a pessimistic view of life. On the 20th, after school, she returned home and spent a week bidding farewell to relatives, friends, and classmates before disappearing. She also sent a letter of farewell to her classmates Li Huanyun, Zhang Wanqing, and Cao Wenlan. After receiving the letter, these students rushed to inform her family, who dispatched people to search in all directions, but without any trace.

Mistaken for Thief, Wrongfully Chopped to Death 103

Chen Erdaizi, a villager from Tangjiazhuang in the sixth district of the county, was passing by Tang Xiaoliuzi's door on his way home the night before last (the 18th) when Tang mistook him for a thief. Tang led Xiaohuaizi and others, wielding knives, and chopped Chen Lianliu to death. Realizing the trouble he had caused, Tang, in an attempt to cover up the crime, hired a cart driver, Tang Yan'er, to dispose of Chen's body in Jiang Xiaozhuang, on the border of Jiangdu and Taixian. Chen's wife, Zhang, noticing that Chen had not returned, inquired with Yang, the wife of villager Tang Huai, and learned of the events. She then discovered Chen's body in Jiang Xiaozhuang and reported it to the Sixth Public Security Branch, which reported it to the Jiangdu Branch Court. Yesterday, Inspector Zhu, along with forensic officials and police officers, went to conduct an examination.

Nantong

Maintaining the Junshan Meteorological Observatory 104

The Junshan Meteorological Observatory was founded by the late gentry Zhang Jian and has achieved considerable results. It is currently affiliated with Nantong College, but its funding is very limited, making it difficult to maintain. The county government specifically submitted a request to the Construction Department for county funds to be allocated for subsidies. On the 23rd, an order was received stating that the observatory's equipment is legitimate, its history is long, and its achievements are commendable. It is rare to have such a foundation in a private meteorological observatory in the country. The request to allocate 600 yuan annually from the county's construction funds and agricultural improvement funds to maintain the observatory is approved, starting from January 1934. It is stipulated that the observatory must send the results of meteorological tests conducted at 6:00 AM and 2:00 PM daily to the Construction Department for comparison and should provide the test results to meet the needs of construction and agriculture as much as possible. Special attention should be paid to reporting typhoons and high tides in summer and autumn.

Mao Zuquan Goes to Chuan Port to Bury His Mother 105

Mao Zuquan, President of the Administrative Court, escorted his mother's coffin from Beijing back to Tongzhou. A memorial service was held at the Xisi Temple, and mourners from both sides of the Yangtze River and Li Leng, the magistrate of Chuansha County, came to Tongzhou to pay their respects. On the 24th, Mao returned to Chuan Port for the burial. Furthermore, his eldest son, Shengxuan, was shot and killed in Shanghai by Korean vagrants in 1920. His coffin has also been transported to Nantong for burial together.

Hangzhou

Hotel Owner's Wife Hangs Herself 106

Chen Changming, a native of Zhuji, 26 years old, residing at No. 240 Buhefang Road, Hangzhou, opened the Changchun Garden Hotel there. It has been nearly a month since its opening. He partnered with someone surnamed He, with Chen Changming's wife, Ms. Zhan, taking care of the store, hoping to develop the business with a beautiful woman tending the stove. Unexpectedly, things did not go as planned, and the business was sluggish, resulting in significant losses. Chen Changming planned to close the store and take his wife back to his hometown, but Ms. Zhan refused, leading to a quarrel. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday, at 7:30 PM, she went upstairs and hanged herself. She was discovered, but it was too late to save her.

Yi Chengen, Chief of the Fifth Public Security Bureau of Yixing County, cracked down on a reactionary organization on the morning of the 20th at Zhongxin An Elementary School in Zhangzhu, successively arresting six people including Guo Xiheng (aka Yin Wu), Wang Qixian, Hua Yaqiang, and Mei Xingsheng. That night, the County Public Security Bureau also arrested a young woman named Bao Yuehua in the Wenchang Palace in the urban area. Jiaxing

Salt Police Harass Villagers 108

Mo Sihai, Shen Wencai, and other farmers in Baihuazhuang Sanhewan, Tanghui Town, Jiaxing, make pickled vegetables every winter and sell them in various places in the spring. Currently, they are in the process of pickling vegetables. The day before yesterday, Zhu, the deputy captain of the First Team of the Jiahu Commercial Affairs Anti-Smuggling Camp, led salt police and forcibly claimed that the salt used by Mo and Shen for pickling vegetables was smuggled salt. They forced them to pay a fine of one hundred and four yuan, tied up the villagers with ropes, and detained them in the Baihuazhuang Temple. Eventually, they were forced to pay the fine, and sixteen jars of official salt were confiscated. It was found that the salt stored by the villagers was purchased from the Tongrun Sauce Garden in Tanghui and they had invoices from the garden as proof. However, the salt police arbitrarily made false accusations and extorted huge sums of money, showing a complete disregard for the law. Currently, more than ten township offices in the area are appealing to the All-Zhejiang Public Association, requesting them to uphold justice and petition the salt administration authorities to order an investigation to deter the illegal activities and reassure the farmers.

Xiaoshan

Night Boat Robbed En Route 109

The night boat from Shaoxing to Xiaoshan, near Suoqian in Xiaoshan, was robbed by three pirate boats while sailing to Xixiaojiang on the night of the 22nd. All the cloth and silver dollars, worth about 500 yuan, were looted. A'Yuan, a crew member, was slashed in the foot by a pirate's knife, causing profuse bleeding and unconsciousness. The crew member has been taken to Linpu Hospital for treatment, and the county has been notified to assist in the arrest of the robbers.

Zhang Ji and Others Expected to Arrive in Shanghai This Morning 110

Traveling to Beijing Tonight

Central Government to Hold Important Meeting

In order to expedite the entry of Central Committee members from the Southwest into Beijing to attend the Fourth Plenary Session and to solicit opinions on resolving the Fujian Incident, the Central Government dispatched Zhang Ji, Ma Chaojun, Wang Luyi, Chen Zhaoying, and four others to Hong Kong on the 9th of this month to meet with Hu Hanmin.
