Shen Yi Discusses Developing Greater Shanghai 111

Recently, the Municipal Government and its affiliated bureaus have been busy relocating, and it is expected that they can all move into the new municipal center area by the end of this month. A reporter from the Central News Agency specially went to the old site of the Municipal Bureau of Public Works to visit Director Shen Yi and inquire about his opinions on developing Greater Shanghai in the future. He was received and the conversation went as follows:

Primary Steps: Shen believes that completing the construction of Greater Shanghai should be divided into several steps. We are currently in a time of national crisis, and the city's economy is also very difficult. It is not easy to make active progress. In the past few years, the municipal authorities have painstakingly planned the construction of Greater Shanghai, and it was confirmed at that time that developing the city center area was the primary step in promoting the Greater Shanghai plan. After several years of efforts, the main roads in the city center area have been gradually completed, and the new municipal government building and temporary houses for various bureaus have also been completed. All staff will be able to move into the new buildings for office work soon.

Prosperity Plans: Shen's efforts to prosper the city center area focus on the driving forces of prosperity. The relocation of the Municipal Government and its affiliated bureaus is not as important as building the Qiujiang Wharf, opening a commercial port, and relocating the train station, but Shen believes that the relocation of the Municipal Government is also one of the driving forces for the prosperity of the city center area. As for building the wharf and other matters, they are indeed important driving forces, but implementing such projects may not be permitted by the current environment. After the Municipal Government and various bureaus relocate, they will pay attention to another driving force, such as libraries, museums, and sports fields, all of which are necessary constructions for the prosperity of the city. Shen feels that with the current financial constraints of the city, construction cannot be carried out simultaneously, and all municipal buildings will be given priority in the city center area, based on the city's financial capacity.

Citizen Cooperation: Shen also stated that while the municipal authorities will do their best to develop the city center area, they also expect all citizens of the city, whether in the banking or industrial and commercial sectors, to invest in the city center area as a priority or to start businesses, so as to achieve the effect of government-citizen cooperation. The Municipal Government and its affiliated bureaus, and all staff, have become the vanguard of the citizens, moving into the city center area to show the government's determination to prosper the city center area. Shen also informed that although the construction of the city center area is recognized by the Chinese people as a matter of urgency, foreign commentators often criticize it as being merely empty talk. The reason why they make such comments is that the development of the city center area will inevitably deal a great blow to the concessions. Therefore, our citizens should sincerely assist the government to complete the Greater Shanghai plan.

Renovating Old Areas: Shen still believes that the renovation of the old urban area should not be neglected. The renovation of the old urban area will be based on a stable approach. In the past, after the Dongmen Street of Xiaodongmen and the Heping Road of Laoximen were developed, the market in those areas immediately became prosperous. In the future, the attitude of caution will be adopted in opening roads. He has many plans for renovating the old urban area, but they are often limited by funding and subject to other constraints, so they have not been realized sooner. The streets in the old urban area are mostly rugged and uneven and should be repaired quickly to facilitate pedestrian traffic. The ditches have been in disrepair for a long time and lack a system, and they will also be renovated.

Min Bandits' Initial Plan for Alliance of Offense and Defense Broken by National Army 120

Red Bandit Front Collapses After Guangze is Recovered

Forced Recruitment of Civilians in Southern Fujian Has Aroused Resentment

Xinsheng News Agency reports that the great battle on the border of Zhejiang and Fujian is about to break out. Yesterday, a local agency obtained information from the front, stating that the vanguard troops of the Fujian side launched a full-scale attack from Taishun and Qingyuan. The Central Army has made thorough arrangements. The Taishun line is a rugged mountain path, suitable only for lightly armed troops and not for large armies with sufficient light and heavy equipment. Once the great battle begins, the Fujian army will be completely annihilated. However, the Fujian army knows that if the Central Government mobilizes the sea, land, and air forces simultaneously, it will be unable to resist. Therefore, it still relies on an alliance of offense and defense with the red bandits, attempting to increase its strength and deliberately using the dangerous mountain roads, along with the red bandits' tactics of dispersing to avoid immediate annihilation, to prolong the war. The first step in the plan of the Fujian army and the red bandits is to have the red bandits leave Shangrao in Jiangxi, pass through Guangfeng, and attempt to attack Changshan and Yushan to directly impact Quzhou in eastern Zhejiang, intending to cut off the Central Army on the Fujian-Zhejiang border. However, this conspiracy was discovered by the Central Army on the front line, which moved first. Then the □□□ unit of the Central Army launched a head-on attack in Guangze, cutting the bandit army in half. One group fled into Zhejiang, and the other was defeated and collapsed in Jiangxi. The previous rumors in this city about the battle in eastern Zhejiang were actually this battle in which the bandits and the Fujian side colluded internally and externally. However, it has now completely failed. In addition, according to intelligence reports, in addition to buying over the bandits led by Fan Tiemin in Shouning, the Fujian rebels are also actively reorganizing local militias, bandits, and knife gangs in the rear of Fujian Province to fill the so-called People's Self-Defense Army. However, due to incomplete equipment and lack of funding, they cannot form an army. However, it is worth noting that the Fujian rebels are colluding with the communists and completely lifting the blockade. Therefore, the bandit side has recently purchased a large amount of salt and goods in Fuzhou and transported them to bandit areas through Yangkou, Shunchang, Jiangle, and Taining to provide the red bandits with material needs. At the same time, the Fujian puppet government, seeing the difficulty in organizing the militia, is forcibly recruiting people from the people in southern Fujian. Families with three or more able-bodied men must send one person to serve as a reserve force. The people are forced by the coercion and are mostly brewing resistance. The fact that they cannot win the support of the people is evident. Therefore, no one believes in the deceptive slogan of "distributing land according to population". Although Zhangzhou, Xiamen, and Minhou are seemingly still calm on the surface, their internal instability is growing. The future of the so-called People's Government is bleak.

All Silk Factories in This City Shut Down 121

Total of More Than 60,000 Unemployed Workers

Due to Japanese Silk Invasion and Rural Bankruptcy

Silk is originally a major export product of our country. However, in recent years, one reason is the bankruptcy of rural areas in the country, and the other is the brisk sales of Japanese silk in Europe and the United States, resulting in a continuous decrease in the export of silk from our country. A reporter from Xinxin News Agency learned from the silk industry in this city yesterday that Shanghai originally had 65 silk factories. Recently, due to the plummeting price of silk, it has been difficult to maintain operations. In the past month, 63 factories have successively announced their closure. The remaining two factories are also in dire straits. The number of silk workers who have lost their jobs will also reach 60,000. This phenomenon has a great impact on the future of the silk industry and social security. It is heard that the National Economic Committee, in view of this, will organize a Silk Industry Control Committee to collect materials on the causes of the decline of the silk industry in the past in order to decide on steps for improvement and relief.

Manufacturers Petition for Tax Exemption 122

Hopes to Achieve the Goal

Before the implementation of the tax collection, the flour manufacturers in this city, Fuxin, Fufeng, and Xinda, ordered wheat from various countries, totaling 24 ships, of which nine ships were directly ordered from the Cotton and Wheat Office of the Economic Committee, and two ships were sold by foreign merchants, all with tax guarantees from the Economic Committee, which should not be a problem. However, the remaining 13 ships were ordered by the manufacturers from local foreign merchants such as Quanlong, Xiangmao, and Lieji, which is a large amount. They have repeatedly discussed with the Ministry of Finance authorities to request tax exemption. Shen Shuyu from the Customs Administration came to Shanghai and scheduled to meet with representatives of the manufacturers yesterday. The details of the meeting and Shen's attitude are recorded as follows:

Yesterday Morning's Consultation 123

At 9:30 yesterday morning, Gu Xinyi, the leading representative of the manufacturers, went to Shen's residence to discuss the tax exemption situation. Shen proposed a certain opinion, and tax exemption was quite difficult. After Gu repeatedly explained the difficulties faced by the flour manufacturers in recent years, hoping that they would understand the difficulties of the business, Shen also expressed his sympathy. However, the Ministry of Finance has already issued an order, which seems difficult to exempt. However, the purpose of this tax increase is to protect domestic farmers and cannot increase the burden on industry and commerce. Shen promised to consult with the Minister of Finance before making a decision. It is expected that after another negotiation, the goal of tax exemption can be achieved.

Foreign Wheat Arrived in Shanghai 124

One ship of foreign wheat, about 8,000 tons, arrived yesterday. Two ships will be loaded today, and the remaining ships will arrive around the end of the month. The flour manufacturers stated that if the goal is not achieved, they will not unload the goods for the time being to show their determination. The foreign merchants who sell this foreign wheat are also quite anxious and hope to resolve the issue as soon as possible.

Expected to be Resolved 125

This time, in addition to the 11 ships of American wheat borrowed, there are a total of 13 ships of foreign wheat, totaling more than 110,000 tons, which have been registered with the Social Affairs Bureau. If taxes are collected according to the tax rate, the total tax amount will be more than 800,000 yuan. According to Gu Xinyi's statement to the Shenshi News Agency, at this time of financial constraints, there are many places where the government needs the assistance of manufacturers, and the government cannot bear to protect farmers at the expense of businesses. It is expected that after another one or two negotiations, a satisfactory solution can be achieved.

Municipal Government Relocates to New Building 127

Various Bureaus Officially Relocate Today

Celebration Ceremony to be Held on New Year's Day

The various bureaus under the Municipal Government have officially ceased operations from today and have begun to relocate to the new building in the city center area. The Municipal Government is also in the process of relocating. Due to the relocation, the various bureaus will not be able to operate effectively during the year. A large-scale celebration will be held on New Year's Day. The details are recorded as follows:

Relocation Begins Today 128

The various bureaus under the Municipal Government began to relocate today. (1) The Land Bureau moved to its new address today and will be completed in about three days. The bureau has very few rooms at the new address, and the drawing room of the Third Section is not enough to arrange, so it will remain at the original site of Yesiyuan for office work. The city's grain cabinet originally borrowed civilian houses. Now that it has been relocated, the original old bureau site will be temporarily used for the grain cabinet to work. (2) The Social Affairs Bureau also officially moved today. After the relocation, three or four people will be temporarily left at the original site of Dananmen to receive and send documents and contact affairs. As for the original houses, they originally belonged to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. How to deal with them in the future is still uncertain. Most of them may be returned to the landlord, leaving one or two rooms for office use, which is also unknown. (3) The Health Bureau also moved today and has set up an office at the Nanshi Clinic on Penglai Road. Public affairs such as school health and street cleaning will be handled by the office. It is also planned to choose a location on the original site of the Land Bureau or the Social Affairs Bureau for the establishment of the Nanshi Hospital, which is currently being discussed separately. (4) The Education Bureau has wrapped up all the documents of the various sections a few days ago and is scheduled to relocate all of them on the 26th. It is planned not to set up a separate office. (5) The Bureau of Public Works has actually moved in gradually due to various construction projects in the city center area. From today, all documents and equipment have also been largely moved in. (6) The Municipal Government is scheduled to officially move in on the 28th. (7) The Bureau of Public Utilities, the Bureau of Finance, and the Bureau of Public Safety will temporarily remain in their old locations because the houses have not been built. However, the Bureau of Public Safety previously had a plan to move to the original site of Shanghai County, but now that the houses there have not been repaired, it is uncertain when it can be realized.

Establishing Joint Office 129

The city center area is a newly created central area, located on the riverside, with a secluded scene, very different from the bustling city area. However, most citizens are gathered in southern Shanghai and cannot follow the Municipal Government to leave. In the future, in order to facilitate contact affairs on all sides, the Municipal Government and various bureaus plan to set up offices. However, the municipal bureaus are planning independently, which is not conducive to centralized office work, and the expenditure is also considerable. Previously, someone proposed that each bureau set up a joint office within the Municipal Government office. Whether it can be realized in the future, whether the address is at the old site of the Municipal Government at Fenglin Bridge, and whether it is necessary for each bureau to set up an office will be formally decided after another meeting.

Exchange of Customs Duty Treasury Bills 132

Ministry of Finance Announces Extension to June of Next Year

The Ministry of Finance announced that the exchange of old customs duty short-term treasury bills with a fixed amount of 50 million yuan from the 19th year of the Republic for new bills with a revised fixed amount of 80 million yuan, which had previously been extended to the end of this month, will be suspended. In an instant, the deadline has arrived again, but the number of bill holders in various places requesting an exchange is still small. It is learned that the Ministry of Finance, in consideration of the convenience of bill holders, has specially extended the period for another six months, until June 30th of the 23rd year of the Republic. All holders of these old bills must exchange them for new bills at the local Central, China, and Communications Banks within the deadline.

Shipping Companies Jointly Raise Funds to Build a Yantai Dockyard 133

Surveying Stone Grandmother Estuary

Actively Underway

Regaining Shipping Rights

The power of Chinese shipping in China, with China Merchants as the largest in the south, and Zhengji leading in the north, hence the saying "China Merchants in the South, Zhengji in the North". However, Zhengji's ships mostly hire Japanese senior crew members, and because there are no domestic dockyards in the north, each year when the ships enter the factory for repairs, contracts are also signed with Japanese dockyards. This not only allows rights to flow out, but also hinders shipping administration. The Tianjin Shipping Administration Bureau learned that Zhengji's dockyard contract with the Japanese will expire in April next year. Xu Daxing, the director of the Yantai Shipping Bureau, has repeatedly consulted with Zhang Zhengben, the owner of Zhengji, requesting that he not renew the lease after the contract expires, abolish the contract, and instead enter a domestic shipyard. However, there is no complete dockyard in North China, and going to Shanghai is inconvenient. Therefore, after consultation, it was decided to establish a large dockyard in Yantai to meet the needs of North China's merchant ships, starting with government supervision and commercial operation. The first step is to survey the location and purchase land. This project has been submitted to the Ministry for approval, which has been forwarded to the Shandong Provincial Government to instruct the Yantai Administrative Commissioner to jointly prepare for and proceed with the project. Since this matter concerns shipping rights, it is urgently investigated and recorded as follows:

Motivation for Building a Dockyard 134

Xu Daxing, the director of the Yantai Shipping Bureau, believes that Zhifu and Longkou are the most developed areas for transportation in the north, and Zhengji Company's general management office is located in Yantai. Other shipping lines such as Huitong, Hexing, Fuxing, and Northern also have significant operations. Furthermore, many merchant ships from other domestic locations navigate to Yantai. In total, there are forty to fifty ships owned and managed on regular schedules. However, the most necessary dockyard for ships has not yet been established. Each time the ships encounter major or minor repairs, they often sail to Dalian, Lushun, or south to Hong Kong, Kowloon, or even east to Japan. The outflow of rights is a great pity. Therefore, the construction of a dockyard in Yantai is a matter of great urgency.

Impact on Fishery 135

Without dockyard equipment, if the machine platform fails during shipping administration, it is difficult to repair it immediately and continue sailing, so the authority of the Shipping Bureau cannot be strictly enforced. Furthermore, Yantai is an important fishing area in North China. According to the Premier's industrial plan, it is an important fishing port. There are currently dozens of fishing vessels, and most of the annual repairs and new construction are also handled in Japan or Dalian. Therefore, the establishment of a dockyard directly recovers shipping rights and indirectly promotes the fishing industry.

Government Supervision and Commercial Operation 136

The establishment of a dockyard in Yantai cannot be delayed, and it must be realized in the short term. Now, after consultation, the establishment of a dockyard is nothing more than three types: government-run, government-business joint venture, and government-supervised commercial operation. If the government invests in construction, the scale can be grand, but it is feared that there will be no time for this. It has been decided to proceed with the government-supervised commercial operation plan first. Xu Daxing has repeatedly invited various shipping companies in Yantai to hold meetings and consultations, and Zhengji Company originally leased land from the Japanese government in Dalian to establish a private dockyard, which will expire in April next year. They were advised not to renew the lease after the expiration, and to jointly establish a large dockyard with various shipping bureaus, which was unanimously agreed upon. However, it is necessary to request government assistance to proceed.

Surveying the Location 137

The suitable location for building a dockyard in Yantai has been surveyed at the Stone Grandmother Estuary in the southeast of Zhifu Island. The coast there is more than a thousand feet above sea level. During the thirteenth year of the Republic, it was contracted to local people by the Yantai Official Property Clearance Office at a price of two yuan per mu. However, it is heard that the payment has not been made, and only a license from the Official Property Office has been obtained, but not a ministerial license. The people have not obtained legal property rights. Recently, it was heard that they plan to build a dockyard there and are engaging in speculation, raising the land price more than two hundred times. There are still problems with purchasing the land.

Government Assistance 138

Since the people are making such demands, the government should transfer the matter to the local government and send personnel to investigate. The coast belongs to the state and should be taken back at the purchase price. The nearby land should be fairly evaluated. The matter has been approved by the Ministry of Communications and forwarded to the Shandong Provincial Government to instruct the Yantai District Administrative Commissioner to jointly handle the matter. Each transfer will be handled separately. Another Yantai construction office will be established and implemented.

Tax Exemption on Materials 139

At the beginning of the establishment, all construction funds will be filled by shipping companies. However, at the beginning of the establishment, a request was made to the Ministry of Finance to approve tax exemptions for machinery and materials purchased from foreign countries for the site, which can reduce costs and avoid competition from foreign merchants. The Ministry of Communications has already instructed that since merchants are willing to invest in construction, the government will do its best to support them. Currently, the matter is being expedited. It is expected that within a year, the large Yantai dockyard in North China can be completed, and thereafter, domestic merchant ships will no longer need to enter Japanese shipyards.

Workers on Both Wusong Factory Lines Decide to Resume Work This Morning 140

Ban Moheng Awaits Processing

Ministry Member Returns to Report Today

The Dagong News Agency reports that all workers at the Wusong Zhanghuabang machine factory and materials department, due to Ban Moheng's destruction of the labor movement, demanded that the bureau dismiss and investigate him, and declared a work slowdown starting on the 18th of this month. After the Central Organization Committee and the Ministry of Railways sent personnel to Shanghai to mediate, a considerable result has been achieved. The workers are scheduled to resume work uniformly starting this morning. Since the work slowdown at the Wusong machine factory and materials department, the party departments and labor unions on both lines have sent personnel to persuade them, but to no avail due to the workers' firm will. The Central Organization Committee and the Ministry of Railways sent personnel to Shanghai to handle the matter. At 5 PM the day before yesterday, they met with Wang Bi, Yuan Boyang, Lu Baogan of the Railway Bureau, Chen Chengshi, Li Dasan of the Party Departments on both lines, and Min Luobi of the Labor Union, etc., and went to Wusong to convene all foremen and section chiefs of the Wusong factory office to discuss solutions and provide persuasion. It was finally decided that the Ministry of Railways would be responsible for thoroughly investigating the Ban Moheng matter, and all workers should resume work first. Each person, in order to comply with the advice of higher authorities, expressed acceptance, and held a workers' congress at 7 AM yesterday morning, deciding to resume normal work at 6 AM this morning. The Ban Moheng matter will be submitted to the authorities for strict investigation.

Monitoring at Wusong The authorities are deeply concerned that there may be misunderstandings when the workers resume work this morning. Returning to Beijing to Report The counselors of the Ministry of Railways, Wenbin and Zhang Weici, and Luo Meihuan, director of the General Affairs Department of the Central Organization Committee, who were ordered to come to Shanghai to handle the labor unrest at the Wusong machine factory, have come to a conclusion. After inspecting the resumption of work in Wusong this morning, they are scheduled to take a train back to Beijing this afternoon to report their mission. Regarding the workers' accusations against Ban Moheng, they will request instructions after returning to Beijing and then handle the matter.

We should have waited quietly for a decision, but recently, the refugee representatives of the Sui counties have reported additional facts about Cunhou's abandonment of Sui and Xuan counties, which were not fully presented in the previous telegram. Therefore, we sent Comrade Li Yansheng to Beijing to present our sincere feelings in person. I will first summarize the main points and ask for your inspection. Liu Cunhou usually squeezes the people's wealth, exhausting his cruel methods. When he was about to withdraw, he levied a huge amount of more than one million on the four counties in the name of suppressing the bandits. The army went out to press and urge the payment. At that time, the people still hoped that he would resist the bandits and endured the pain without speaking out. However, once the Sui army fled wildly, the hundreds of thousands of people's houses and tombs were offered to the bandits. What is even more hateful is that when Cunhou withdrew from the south gate of Suicheng, tens of thousands of refugees crowded at the city gate. Cunhou ordered the soldiers to kill a way out, and hundreds of people were killed and injured. When he reached the floating bridge across the Qu River, the people followed one after another. Cunhou reached the opposite bank and ordered it to be cut off, and hundreds of people fell into the river and died. His heart is more cruel than the bandits. This should be combined and punished together. Cunhou has a large number of guns and ammunition in his storage. When the bandits were in short supply, the people of Sui and Xuan requested to borrow thousands of guns to help suppress the bandits, but he was stingy and did not give them. When he was about to withdraw, he sent representatives to plead and temporarily keep the troops as a backing, allowing the teams to act as vanguards, but he ignored them. He willingly held 7,000 to 8,000 guns and 4 to 5 million bullets in storage, according to Liu Bangjun himself. Handing over to the bandits, the people did not ask for them to be issued, and the army did not transport them when they withdrew. The crime of misleading the people is small, but the crime of helping the bandits is great. This should be combined and strictly punished. Cunhou has already hidden in Chongqing and is about to enter the province. We earnestly ask you to clearly order the arrest and trial. The association is willing to send personnel to confront each other. If it is false, we are willing to accept the crime of false accusation. Furthermore, Liu Bangjun was originally the commander of the First Division of the army. When the bandits invaded Sichuan, the Sui defense was disturbed. Bangjun should have led his troops to the battlefield to command and fulfill his duties. However, in the name of a representative, he went to the province last fall and stayed for a year. When the order to accept the troops was issued, if he had any bloodiness, he should have rushed to the place where the troops were concentrated to reorganize them day and night. Now, it is heard that the five-way army is unanimously advancing to suppress the bandits, but he secretly went to Chongqing and invites people from the military, political, and news circles in Zhang Qiuyongnianchun Restaurant, fabricating facts to cover up the ugly traces of his troops' retreat without fighting. With such behavior, how can he be expected to make amends for his sins? Moreover, the army has been stationed in Sui for ten years, and resentment has accumulated. The people have long sighed that they will die together. If Bangjun is allowed to accept his troops again, and they are still stationed there after Suixuan is recovered, it will inevitably lead to civil unrest. The pain this time has been deep, how can we allow the army to burn the beans again to fry them? We earnestly ask you to investigate and approve the dismissal of Bangjun from his military post to save the remnant. As for the army, there may be useful people, and we also ask Commander Liu Xiang to reorganize and dismiss them, using it as a prelude to reducing troops and saving military expenses, and completing the great plan of political unification as soon as possible. I will wait for orders in camp. Furthermore, the refugees of Suixuan who have fled to neighboring counties number hundreds of thousands. At the end of the year and the cold weather, food and clothing are difficult. We earnestly ask Commander Liu Xiang to recover Suixuan by the deadline so that the refugees can return to their homeland as soon as possible. Otherwise, the tragic situation of displacement will worsen day by day, and there are unimaginable consequences. We have a straightforward nature and know how to take care of ourselves. We rarely discuss military and political affairs. Recently, we have received telegrams from refugees urging us to speak out to the authorities. We are concerned about our homeland and cannot ignore it. We have submitted them repeatedly. It is not our intention. We are weeping and asking for orders, and we hope that you will consider and adopt them. Then, the millions of people in Suixuan will all wear the virtue of rebirth. In addition to the personal presentation by Representative Li, we have prepared a document for your review and approval, and respectfully present it to the Chairman of the National Government Lin, the President of the Executive Yuan Wang, and the Chairman of the Military Commission Jiang.

Guangdong Provincial Government Consults the Ministry of Finance to Quickly Resolve the Qinlian Cane Sugar Case 143

Consultation Document Delivered to Pang Songhui to Present to the Ministry of Finance in Person

Guangdong is a province that produces a lot of sugarcane in our country. The green sugar of Chaomei, the red sugar of Qiongya, and the white sugar of Lianzhou are all famous. Unfortunately, most of them are made using traditional methods and have not been improved. There have been a few counties that have used machines to make sugar, such as Dongguan, Hepu, and Lingshan. Recently, the province has been vigorously implementing a three-year administration plan, striving to revitalize the sugar industry. Recently, the Construction Department prepared the headquarters of the five major sugar factories, and the military reclamation area also prepared to establish a sugar factory. It also dispatched eighteen technicians to the Philippines to study sugar refining. The provincial government also hired two American sugar experts as sugar industry consultants, with a desire to catch up quickly. Unexpectedly, the emerging sugar industry plan has not yet been realized, and the original local sugar exported from Qinlian and other places to Shanghai was repeatedly fined and confiscated by the Jianghai Customs, resulting in suspension of operations. This case caused a sensation throughout the province. People from all walks of life generally believe that this is a fatal blow to the province's agricultural, commercial, and economic sectors. Letters and telegrams have been sent calling for relief, but the government has not resolved the matter after several months of delay. This time, Pang Songhui, the representative of the Qinlian sugar merchants, went to Guangzhou to petition. The Southwest authorities expressed outrage and tried their best to provide relief. The provincial government prepared a consultation document and handed it to Representative Pang to take to Beijing to present to the Ministry of Finance in person, requesting that it be investigated and resolved quickly in order to maintain domestic products. The consultation document from the Guangdong Provincial Government to the Ministry of Finance is as follows: For the matter of consultation, it is currently reported by Liao Zhuzhou, chairman of the Beihai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and Tan Qiaonan, chairman of the Hepu County Chamber of Commerce, etc., that according to a letter from the Qinlian Sugar Industry Guangyi Hall, it said, "We have received letters from our colleagues Heli, Henghalong, Guangchanghe, Heyi, etc., stating that from July to September of this year, our colleagues shipped local white sugar from Beihai to Shanghai five times. Each time, they reported to the Beihai Customs for inspection and confirmed that it was pure local sugar. They paid the transit tax in accordance with the regulations before they were released. Unexpectedly, when the original shipment arrived in Shanghai, it was completely detained by the Jianghai Customs Tax Affairs Department, claiming that it was mixed with 10% to 20% foreign sugar, and a total of 1,560 yuan was fined and 1,957 yuan was supplemented. The method used to distinguish between local sugar and foreign sugar has no standard and is prone to errors. Our colleagues have jointly submitted a telegram to appeal in the case, but it has not been resolved after more than a month. Our colleagues are innocent and have suffered a major loss, forcing us to temporarily suspend operations pending relief." A list of fines for each company is attached for verification, and we request that the Beihai Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Qinlian County Chambers of Commerce be forwarded to the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance, ordering the Jianghai Customs Tax Affairs Department to issue the fines in full to show fairness, etc. We have examined that Beihai is an important port for the export of local sugar in South China, and the Beihai Customs is close to the sugar-producing area, and has a clear understanding of the composition of local sugar and the difference from foreign sugar. Therefore, our colleagues have reported and attached local sugar in the past, and they have all been inspected and released without any misunderstandings. Now, the original shipment has arrived in Shanghai, and the Jianghai Customs has identified it as mixed with foreign sugar and imposed a large fine, which is obviously abusing its power and destroying local sugar. If it is not stopped in accordance with the law, how can farmers and merchants be able to settle down? Therefore, we have recorded the case and reported it, and we request that it be forwarded to alleviate the merchants' difficulties, etc., as approved. We have examined that since the Jianghai Customs deducted and fined the local sugar case, sugar merchants have stopped transporting, resulting in considerable losses, and the farmers and workers in more than ten towns who rely on the sugar industry to make a living are likely to lose their jobs and go bankrupt. Livelihood and security are greatly affected. The letter was previously approved, and we will take this matter as a matter of livelihood for more than ten towns of farmers and merchants, and we will jointly convene the sugar industry and other trade associations, and all sugar merchants, to discuss relief measures. A total of four items were discussed and decided: (1) Please the Ministry of Finance to correct the erroneous method of the Jianghai Customs for inspecting the difference between local sugar and foreign sugar. (2) Please the Ministry of Finance to order the Jianghai Customs to release the local sugar of the Beihai sugar merchants and return the fines and tax supplements collected in the past. (3) Please the Executive Yuan to order the customs offices throughout the country to protect the safety of local sugar imports and exports, and not to deliberately delay. (4) Please the Central Government to clearly exempt local sugar from export and transit taxes, and to set up a local sugar export incentive program. It was unanimously passed, in addition to telegrams and separate reports, we have specifically recorded the case and reported it to your government, and we have publicly appointed Pang Songhui as a representative to personally present everything. We still hope that you will cherish the hundreds of thousands of sugar farmers and merchants in Qinlian and other places who are in a situation of unemployment and provide special relief, and separately forward them to the Executive Yuan, and consult the Ministry of Finance to adopt and implement the above four items as much as possible. The Qinlian sugar industry is fortunate, and the national industry is fortunate, etc. In view of this, the matter concerns the transportation and sales of local sugar and the revitalization of domestic industry and commerce, and we request your ministry to investigate and handle it. In addition to replying, we should consult and still look forward to seeing the restoration, to connect with public friendship, this consults the Ministry of Finance.

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Works Dredges Zoumatang River 144

The project has now begun

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Works has begun dredging the Zoumatang River. Its plan includes (1) "Desire to End," from Xiaojipu west to the 26th section west of Lingnan Road; (2) "Length," 4,159 meters; (3) "Width," the width of the new riverbed is tentatively set at 35 meters, to be determined during detailed planning before construction; (4) "Slope," the slope of both banks is set at 1:2, and appropriately changed to 1:1.5 in overly narrow areas; (5) "Earthwork," approximately 92,000 cubic meters; (6) "Expenses," excavation and water removal are expected to cost a total of 25,000 yuan; (7) "Source of Funds," 7,000 yuan from the Jiangwan District's stored water conservancy fees, with the remainder borne by the municipal treasury. The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Works has sent letters to the Jiangwan District Municipal Committee and the Municipal and County Water Conservancy Committee yesterday to investigate.

The City's National Medicine Association Held its Fourth General Assembly Yesterday 154

The List of Elected Executive and Supervisory Committee Members for the Fourth Term Will Be Announced Today

Approximately 700 people, including representatives from the Municipal Party Department, the Bureau of Social Affairs, and members, attended. They passed important resolutions such as building an association hall and the National Medicine Convention. Details are recorded as follows:

Attending Representatives 155

Those who attended yesterday included Mao Yun from the Municipal Party Department, Xiao Yaxiong from the Public Security Bureau, Zhong Ziyi from the Health Bureau, Yan Wenkai from the Bureau of Social Affairs, Dai Dafu from the Shanghai National Medicine Association, Feng Mingzheng from the Foci Pharmacy, Tao Ledong, Secretary of the National Medicine Association, the China Medical College, the Music Society, the Guanghua Medical Journal Society, and members Guo Boliang, He Yunsheng, Ding Zhongying, Xu Xiaopu, Xie Liheng, Cai Yousheng, Zhu Ziyun, Jiang Wenfang, Zhu Nanshan, Huang Baozhong, Xue Wenyuan, and others, totaling approximately 700 people.

After the ceremony, Xue Wenyuan, Guo Boliang, Xie Liheng, Fu Yongyan, and He Yunsheng were publicly elected as the presidium. Finally, Chairman Xie Liheng delivered a thank-you speech and the meeting adjourned.

Resolutions Passed 157

(1) The proposal to prepare a plan to build the association's hall was passed. (2) The proposal that the association should draft a National Medicine Convention was passed. (3) The proposal that the association should focus on promoting knowledge of national medicine and national drugs was passed and handed over to the next executive committee to handle, with a special publication printed in major newspapers every week. (4) The proposal that anatomy should be added to the curriculum of national medical colleges and vocational schools was passed. (5) The proposal that the resolutions passed by the general assembly must be implemented was passed. (6) The proposal to establish a consultation meeting for difficult and complex cases was passed. (7) The proposal to expand the free clinic for the poor and sick and to help the weak and needy was passed. (8) (Confidential). (9) The resolution to ban witches and spirit mediums from indiscriminately issuing magical prescriptions in order to protect human lives was passed and resolved to be handed over to the next executive committee to send a letter to the competent authorities to ban them. (10) The proposal that the elected officials of the association in this term should take office on time or notify the association of their taking office, otherwise it would be considered abandonment, was passed.

National Medicine Convention 158

The eighteen articles of the National Medicine Convention passed yesterday are as follows: (A) Regarding oneself: (1) Do not be boastful and arrogant, and lose the attitude of a scholar. (2) Do not make exaggerated advertisements and do not engage in unethical profiteering. (B) Regarding patients: (3) When asked to see a patient in an emergency, one should arrive as soon as possible within one's ability. (4) Serious cases in the outpatient clinic should be treated in advance and not be required to wait in line. (5) Convenience should be provided to the poor and sick. (6) Do not be stern and harsh, and do not prescribe prescriptions carelessly, violating the spirit of benevolence. (7) Do not spread people's hidden illnesses and do not perform abortions. (C) Regarding colleagues: (8) When treating patients, do not attack the prescriptions of previous doctors. (9) Do not criticize the shortcomings of colleagues to patients. (10) When consulting with colleagues, be humble and consult with each other, and do not argue and stubbornly insist on one's own opinions. (11) If colleagues have disputes that cannot be resolved, they should report to the association for handling. (12) The purpose of national medical organizations and associations is to provide mutual assistance, communication, and protection of the interests of members. All local national doctors must join the association and abide by the convention. (D) Regarding academics: (13) Trends are new, and we should encourage ourselves to study diligently, study carefully, integrate new knowledge, and promote and develop our profession. (14) The acupuncture, trauma, and surgery of national medicine have remarkable effects. Unfortunately, they have been lost in modern times. It concerns the entire survival of national medicine. We should all strive to promote, publicize secret traditions, so that in the future, the country's administrative hygiene and military rescue services will have a place for national medicine. (15) In one's spare time after seeing patients, one should use what one has learned to promote medicine and hygiene. (16) There are many secret Chinese remedies that have been lost. In the future, they should be made public and various medical publications should be prepared to spread them widely. (17) Those who have no foundation in national medicine, imitate the superficialities of Western medicine, and boast of themselves as national medical scientists, their theories and prescriptions are neither fish nor fowl, and should be corrected together. (18) Drug names must be commonly used and not use obscure aliases, so as not to cause mistakes.

Election of Executive and Supervisory Committees 159

Yesterday, the general assembly also elected the fourth executive committee and supervisory committee. Yan Yangshan and Chen Fengming were appointed as vote counters. As a result, a total of 279 ballots were cast, with two invalid votes. The list of elected executive committee members was not yet announced as of around 6 p.m. It is planned to be announced today. Yesterday, the entire student body of the Chinese Medical College also performed silk and bamboo music, singing, martial arts, and Peking opera, which were quite wonderful.

The City's Chamber of Commerce Held a General Assembly Yesterday to Lecture on Improving Chinese Bookkeeping 160

Nearly 10,000 People Visited and Attended Lectures

Booklets and Forms Attracted Great Attention

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce publicly displayed improved Chinese bookkeeping in the chamber's meeting room at 2 p.m. yesterday for all sectors to visit. At 4 p.m., a lecture was held, attended by Wang Xiaolai, Sheng Zhuosan, Yan Esheng, and others. Wang Xiaolai, chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, gave an opening speech, and then invited accountant Xu Yongzuo to give a lecture, which lasted for two hours. The audience was not tired throughout. The details are as follows:

Visiting Situation: The visit began in the afternoon, with over 50 types of account books, forms, and charts displayed. Each type had completed examples, and accountants Wu Huirong, Xiong Baozun, Ruan Xiting, Meng Wangqu, Zhang Huanjun, and important staff members Xu Hanqing, Pan Shihao, and Cha Yubo from the Xu Accountant Office provided explanations and guidance at any time. Many people from major commercial institutions in Shanghai, such as the Silk Industry Bank, Wuzhou Pharmacy, and Sanbei Company, went to study in detail one by one. From 1 p.m. to 6 p.m., no less than 10,000 people came to visit, a very grand occasion. Everyone expressed their admiration and appreciation for this improved Chinese bookkeeping.

Lecture Summary: The lecture by accountant Xu Yongzuo is summarized as follows: (1) Necessity of Improvement: (A) Evolution of Chinese Bookkeeping: Our country's arithmetic and accounting system originated very early. The Nine Chapters on the Mathematical Art and the establishment of officials and systems for accounting in government offices throughout the dynasties are recorded in history and can be verified. Bookkeeping was originally sharpened and promoted by arithmetic and accounting. Therefore, its long history can be imagined. The Book of Rites mentions "books and accounts" together, "accounts" meaning accounting, and bookkeeping was naturally something that should be learned when studying. Descending to the Song Dynasty, there was the system of "four-column registers," which made a significant contribution to bookkeeping. The completeness of its rules can be compared to Western double-entry bookkeeping. Chinese bookkeeping was actually completed with the four columns, dating back more than a thousand years. The completion of Western double-entry bookkeeping was only four or five hundred years ago. This is one of the most precious pages in the history of bookkeeping. Unfortunately, in our country, scholars and gentlemen are ashamed to talk about money and profit, and bookkeeping has rarely been requested. Therefore, progress has been very slow for over a thousand years. The transmission from teacher to apprentice often lost the essence, and each place had its own system and each industry its own method, resulting in disorganized organization and unclear rules. Since the introduction of Western-style bookkeeping in the late Qing Dynasty, the new business community competed to admire it, and Chinese bookkeeping was increasingly ignored by bookkeeping scholars. However, its history is deep, its application is wide, and it cannot be completely replaced by Western-style bookkeeping. Therefore, it can still maintain its considerable position today. (B) Advantages of Chinese Bookkeeping: Having examined Chinese bookkeeping, its important advantages can be summarized in four points: (1) Simple theory: Chinese bookkeeping can also be called the cash receipts and payments bookkeeping method. "Receipts" means the income of funds, "payments" means the expenditure of funds. Increases or decreases in assets and changes that need to be recorded can be used as the standard for recording and calculation in order, without the need to explore the principles of debit and credit as in Western-style bookkeeping. (2) Simple method: In various account books, ledgers, and forms, income items are recorded in the "receipts" section, and expenditure items are recorded in the "payments" section. This is the case for recording, posting, and closing accounts, unlike Western-style bookkeeping, which requires determining the nature of debit and credit accounts for transactions. (3) Popular and easy to understand: The Chinese vertical cash receipts and payments bookkeeping method can be understood by anyone who knows a little bit of reading and arithmetic. With a little instruction, they can record accounts, unlike Western-style bookkeeping, which requires a long period of study. (4) Savings in expenses: Paper, brushes, and ink are all made in China, and their prices are cheaper than foreign goods. Accounting personnel can be engaged in accounting after a little training. Various expenses are lower than those of Western-style bookkeeping. (C) Disadvantages of Chinese Bookkeeping: The advantages are as described above, but there are also not a few disadvantages. The main ones are four: (1) There is no fixed classification of accounts, and their nature is often unclear, inconsistent before and after, and there is no unified management. (2) There is no fixed organization of account books, and they are often reversed, disordered, and lack a system. (3) There is no fixed format for account books, ledgers, and forms, and there are no standards to follow when recording. (4) There are no fixed rules for accounting methods, and the recorder is free to do as they please. (D) Necessity of Improving Chinese Bookkeeping: Chinese bookkeeping is the bookkeeping with the longest history and the widest application in China. Since it has its own inherent advantages, its shortcomings should be improved to make it a perfect bookkeeping method. From the standpoint of sorting out national essence and advocating national products, it is also necessary to improve it. (2) Necessity of Improvement: (A) Three Prerequisites for Improvement: There are three prerequisites for the improvement of Chinese bookkeeping: (1) Scientific method: Bookkeeping is a science and must be organized using scientific methods in order to rationalize it. (2) Practical application: Bookkeeping takes practical application as a prerequisite, and the improvement plan must strive for convenience in practical use. (3) Savings in expenses: Accounting affairs cannot directly generate profits, so it is necessary to seek savings in expenses within the possible scope. B. Ten Major Guidelines for Improvement: Based on the above three prerequisites, ten major guidelines for improvement can be obtained: (1) Adopt the principles of modern accounting; (2) Maintain the original cash receipts and payments accounting procedures; (3) Maintain the existing cash receipts and payments accounting methods; (4) Use the four-column settlement method; (5) Determine the characters used to record numbers; (6) Stipulate the account and form formats for Chinese bookkeeping; (7) Determine the method of using seals in accounting; (8) Stipulate a systematic and orderly account classification; (9) Stipulate an organized and systematic account book organization; (10) Stipulate rationalized and disciplined accounting rules. C. Three Characteristics of Improvement: There are three characteristics of the improvement plan: (1) Cash receipts and payments accounting method, that is, all income items are recorded in the "receipts" section of the daily journal, posted to the "clearing ledger," and compiled into the "settlement statement." Expenditure items are recorded in the "payments" section of the daily journal, posted to the "clearing ledger," and compiled into the "payments" section of the "settlement statement." However, the direction of receipts and payments for cash accounts is reversed when posting from the daily journal to the clearing ledger and settlement statement. (2) Simple and unified accounting method: It is possible to avoid using the unified daily journal and general ledger or multiple account books, and there is another simple unified accounting method. (3) Strict four-column settlement algorithm: Its function for checking errors is no different from that of a trial balance, and its function for reporting accounting not only expresses the results of receipts and payments, but also expresses and compares the process of receipts and payments. (3) Improvement Process: A. First Stage: Before 1921, I only knew Western-style accounting and did not bother with Chinese bookkeeping. I used to plan accounting for various companies and always suppressed Chinese bookkeeping and praised Western bookkeeping. B. Second Stage: Between 1922 and 1923, after performing the duties of an accountant for many years, I gradually felt that Western-style bookkeeping was not convenient for the general public. On the one hand, I gradually came into contact with Chinese bookkeeping, and I felt that both needed to be improved. I advocated using Chinese account books, vertical records, and adopting Western-style accounting principles. That is, Western style is the body, and Chinese style is the use. At that time, it was advocated to maintain the vertical recording of Chinese bookkeeping, and the paper should be made in China. However, it was believed that the accounting principles and methods should adopt the spirit of Western style. C. Third Stage: Between 1926 and 1927, I gradually gained some understanding of the investigation and research of Chinese bookkeeping. I admitted that its accounting methods were not completely unreasonable, and its organization was not completely unordered. The shortcoming was that they were uneven. Therefore, I advocated improving Chinese bookkeeping based on China's inherent accounting methods and referring to the principles of Western double-entry bookkeeping. However, because it lacked the convenience of multiple rows or unified accounting, it was considered that it could not be used for large-scale businesses. D. Fourth Stage: In the past three or four years, there have been more and more designs for improving Chinese bookkeeping, and the effectiveness of implementation has gradually become apparent. At the same time, a simple unified accounting method and a strict four-column settlement algorithm were discovered and promoted to large-scale businesses, with remarkable results. Therefore, in order to promote popularization, I planned to compile a standard plan applicable to various industries. Therefore, from this year, I have rejected miscellaneous affairs and focused on this. I have compiled more than 30 types of improved Chinese account books and forms, and have also compiled a "General Introduction to Improved Chinese Bookkeeping" in two books, which were delivered to the Standard Account Books and Documents Manufacturing Office for printing and distribution.

Astonishing Dumping of Foreign Coal 161

200 Million Yuan of National Currency Has Leaked Out in the Past Ten Years

If No Remedial Measures Are Taken, the Future of the Coal Industry Is Worrying

Although China's coal industry has been in a state of sluggish sales due to traffic congestion and high freight rates, the dumping of foreign coal has a significant impact. Losing Life on the Seventh Bamboo 162

Wang Yonggen Died Amidst Laughter

Wang Yonggen, a native of Ningbo, was 46 years old. He worked as a tea server on a certain ship. Yesterday was the Winter Solstice Festival, and he was off work as usual. At around 2 p.m., he went to a friend's house at 672 Tiantong Road to play mahjong. Soon, he needed the "seventh bamboo." The player before him also needed the "fourth and seventh bamboo." The player after him needed the "seventh bamboo" and a "five pairs in a waiting hand." But the "seventh bamboo" never came. Then, Wang Shuigen suddenly drew the "seventh bamboo" himself, collapsing from excitement and laughing out loud. He then fell to the ground and died. The other players were shocked and immediately called the police. An ambulance was called and the body was taken to Tongren Hospital and then transferred to the coroner's office for examination.

Yuan Ludeng and Others Are Planning to Establish the Poyang Coal Mine Company 163

The Mining Area Is Located in Poyang County, Jiangxi

Capital Is 1.6 Million Yuan

| Daily Coal Output Can Reach 1,000 Tons |

Our country's mineral resources were originally very rich, but unfortunately, the Chinese people do not manage them themselves, and most of them are exploited by foreigners. Poyang County, Jiangxi Province, has a large mineral source. Shanghai merchant Yuan Ludeng and others have initiated the establishment of a Poyang Mining Company to carry out large-scale mining. Details are recorded as follows:

Brief History of Operation 164

The mining area is located in the Hongmenkou area of Dongxiang, Poyang County, Jiangxi. It has extremely abundant reserves and is conveniently located, with no transportation difficulties. Originally, local wealthy merchant Fang Rensheng and others applied to the Ministry of Industry and Jiangxi Provincial Department of Industry to raise funds to operate and mine it. However, due to limited capital, the daily output of coal was only 30 to 40 tons. At the beginning of this year, Xie Tianxi, a shareholder of another nearby coal mine company, Poyang Le Coal Mine Company, obtained permission from the Ministry of Industry and signed an agreement with the Mining Department.

Establishing a Company 165

Shanghai merchant Yuan Ludeng, Xie Tianxi, Jiang Bochang, and others believed that it would be a pity if the mine was not operated on a large scale. Therefore, they initiated the establishment of the "Poyang Coal Mine Company." They held a promoters' meeting at 1 Kangle Village, Fuxu Road, in Shanghai some time ago. As a result, the initial capital was set at 1.6 million yuan, and Xie Tianxi, Jiang Bochang, Yuan Ludeng, and others were appointed as members of the preparatory committee. Then, the first meeting of the preparatory committee was held, and Jiang Bochang and Xie Tianxi were re-appointed as standing committee members to organize the preparatory office and actively carry out all matters. Fang Rensheng was also appointed as the resident mine manager. It is estimated that after large-scale mining is implemented in the future, the daily output of coal can reach 500 to 1,000 tons.

Temporary Shelters for the Poor Begin to Receive Needy People 166

Three Locations Reached Over 900 People in One Day

Including Those with Long Hair, Filth, and Smoking Habits

Funding Is Insufficient and We Hope All Sectors Will Contribute

The Shanghai Charity Federation establishes temporary shelters for the poor every severe winter to accommodate the poor, hungry, and cold masses, and disperses them at the beginning of spring the following year. This year's shelters began operating yesterday. Details are noted below:

Opened Yesterday 167

Some time ago, the association, due to the increasingly cold weather, contacted the heads of the Chaozhou Guild Hall, Dawang Temple, and ChaoHui Villa through directors Wang Yiting and Huang Hanzhi, requesting to temporarily use them as temporary shelters for the poor. They will be dispersed when the weather warms up in early spring next year, and the original sites will be cleaned and returned. The heads of the various places, as the matter concerns charity, all agreed, so the shelters were able to open as scheduled yesterday (the 24th).

Number of People Received 168

Yesterday, starting from 9:00 AM, the Dawang Temple, Chaozhou Guild Hall, and Chao Hui Villa began simultaneously receiving people. By 6:00 PM, the total number of people received at the three locations had exceeded 900, which is more than the number received on the opening day last year. This resulted in extreme congestion at the registration and inspection areas.

Condition of the Poor 169

Yesterday, among the poor received, most were orphans, those with no support, and the unemployed. The majority were dressed in filthy clothes with hair as long as artemisia. All were given baths and haircuts by the institution. Among them were some with sunken cheeks and emaciated appearances, addicted to smoking opium. Wang Yiting and Huang Hanzhi, two lay Buddhists, temporarily consulted with Zhou Chuliang, the director of the Shanghai Public Hospital, and arranged for a doctor to come to the institution daily to provide medication for treatment. At the same time, the administrators are engaged in persuasion, so that after being discharged, they will avoid falling back into a life of crime.

Insufficient Funds 170

However, this year, due to the depression of industry and commerce, there are many unemployed, and those seeking shelter will undoubtedly come in droves. This has resulted in a significant shortage of cotton clothing and blankets. Regarding fundraising, this year, due to the depression of industry and commerce, donations have not been very enthusiastic. Therefore, we hope that kind-hearted people in society will quickly understand righteousness and provide universal assistance. Please send all kinds of donations to Renji Hall on Six Malu Road.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Revision of Specific Duty on Iron 173

Current tax rates are as high as 27 percent.

Causing foreign goods to be dumped, iron factories cannot survive

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday submitted a memorial to the Ministry of Finance, stating: "Presenting this memorial regarding a request: On the 22nd of this month, we received a letter from the Iron Industry Association stating, 'Copper and iron are daily necessities for the people. Agricultural and industrial tools, construction materials, all use these as the main raw materials.'"

"Related to people's livelihood and economy, it is extremely important. Our country does not yet have the means of smelting. Usually, we completely rely on imports. Now, at the time of construction, the demand is especially high. The customs tariff has always used 10 percent as the principle for taxation. As for machinery, in order to promote industry, it has been reduced to 5 percent. This is a good law and the intention is beautiful. However, since the 12th year of the Republic of China, the specific duty on various steel raw materials has gradually increased, while the ad valorem duty remains at the old rate. After the gold unit was revised the year before last, the conversion is even greater. Based on the latest tax regulations issued in May of this year, compared with the actual order value, some are levied as high as about 30 percent. This is extremely important to the national economy, people's livelihood, and economic construction. Now, we will list the uneven distribution of burden and the most important aspects in detail. According to Rule 187, scrap iron clippings and other fragments are taxed at 4 jiao and 4 fen of customs gold per dan, which is about 8 jiao and 4 fen in silver. However, the actual price is only about 4 pounds sterling per ton, which is about 3 yuan and 8 jiao in silver per dan. Calculated as a percentage, it must be 22 percent. Also, according to Rule 207, scrap iron and sections cut from new goods are taxed at 5 jiao and 5 fen of customs gold per dan, which is about 1 yuan and 5 fen in silver. However, the price per ton is also only 4 pounds sterling, which is about 3 yuan and 8 jiao in silver per dan. Also, according to Rule 208, old iron scrap iron, only suitable for reproduction, is taxed at 4 jiao and 1 fen of customs gold per dan, which is about 7 jiao and 8 fen in silver. However, the price per ton is only about 3 pounds sterling, which is about 2 yuan and 8 jiao and 5 fen in silver per dan. All are above 27 percent. However, according to Rule 176, short cooked strips, etc., which are taxed based on ad valorem, the fixed rate is still 10 percent. The difference between them"

"Is nearly two times. The tax on whole iron is lighter than that on broken scrap iron. This is the first unfairness. The aforementioned three items of scrap iron, waste iron, broken iron, etc., are all fragments of steel and iron materials, specially used by various iron factories and blacksmith shops to manufacture various light machine parts, ironware, building materials, agricultural and industrial tools, and the needs of the people's daily necessities. The application is most frequent and the sales are widest. However, now the tax is above 20 percent, while according to Rule 214, finished building materials, etc., are only taxed at 15 percent. This means that manufacturing utensils and transporting them to China for sale is taxed less, while the raw materials that have not been made and are broken and old are taxed more. This not only"

"Creates the opportunity for dumping foreign goods, but also makes it impossible for domestic industry to develop and compete. That is, various building materials, machinery, utensils, etc., can never be imitated. Because the raw material tax rate is heavier than the finished product, even if it is made, the cost is heavier. How can it be sold at the same price as foreign goods? It is appropriate that industry is extremely advocated, but it is ultimately useless. This is the second unfairness. Also, according to Rule 183, the tax regulations for new iron bars, etc., have been reduced to 5 jiao of customs gold per dan, which is about 9 jiao in silver. The current price per ton is about 5 pounds sterling, which is about 4 yuan and 8 jiao in silver per dan, worth about 18 percent. However, the sections of Rule 207, scrap and sections cut from new goods, that is, the materials cut from these new goods that are not up to standard, and the materials that are discarded from foreign factories, are completely useless abroad and are shipped to China. However, now the tax is heavier than the complete new goods of raw materials. The contradictions are reversed. This is the most extreme. The intention is to lighten the tax on new goods because they are needed for construction and encourage their import. I do not know that China's industry has not yet developed. Usually, what is needed is mainly broken pieces, which are cheapest and most suitable. Moreover, all alterations to building objects and imitations of iron agricultural tools rely entirely on these broken segments, and what China does not have is taxed heavily, while the example of reducing complete new goods is"

"Unclear of the intention. This is the third unfairness. Furthermore, in terms of the tax rate regulations, the same iron goods should have the same tax rate. Generally speaking, new and complete ones should be heavier than old and broken ones. In terms of needs, the raw materials that are daily necessities should be lighter than the manufactured utensils. Even in terms of protecting industry and commerce and promoting construction, light taxes should be levied on what the country does not produce and relies on to supply everything, in order to promote manufacturing. Heavy taxes should be levied on what domestic industry can produce and is sufficient to prevent dumping, in order to benefit the people's livelihood. Moreover, those taxed ad valorem are mostly rare and uncommon items, so it may be slightly heavier, while those taxed specifically are necessarily daily and commonly seen items, so it should originally be lighter."

"Now, the original and the branch are reversed, making the raw materials on which agriculture, industry, commerce, people's livelihood, and daily necessities rely for manufacturing twice as heavy as complete new goods, and the same iron bars are light on new and complete, but heavy on broken and discarded. This is the fourth unfairness. Furthermore, in terms of actual situation and theory, the steel tax rate was originally 10 percent as the most accurate. Then, for the three items of scrap iron in Rules 187, 207, and 208, since they are necessary for civilian industrial use, the tax should originally be lighter than the new goods in Rule 183, and taxed at 10 percent of the actual price, which is in line with the principle. At most, it should be equal to the finished products in Rule 214, and taxed up to 15 percent, and it must not be more than 50 percent of the new goods in Rule 183, then the budding industry may still have a line of life. Now, at the time of promoting industrial construction, old steel"

"Scrap iron is most frequently used. There is no domestic product, and all rely on imports. It should be the same as millet, beans, cloth and silk, with the same tax rate and extra light. Now, on the contrary, it is cutting its own life, making it impossible to imitate, and advocating for foreign goods. This is the fifth unfairness. There are many other imbalances in the tax regulations on various steel, iron and hardware goods, but these few items are the most important, and they are all related to the main presentation of people's livelihood industry. In recent years, the iron industry has been extremely depressed, which may not be due to heavy taxes. Only because it concerns the national treasury, we have to reluctantly transport it, so we have been accumulating difficulties for a long time, and we have never made a request to reduce taxes. If it is beneficial to the country, we originally did not want to make any requests. However, business is declining day by day, accounts are difficult to collect, and iron factories and handicraftsmen are seen to be collapsing one after another, and there is no room for survival. Profit rights are overflowing, and leakage is increasing day by day. There is no way to save it. Even the various handicraftsmen, the utensils and tools needed by the agricultural and industrial workers, must also rely on foreign goods. Even the slightest of a knife and a chisel can hardly be made by themselves, let alone others. As a result, there are more and more unemployed, the customs are declining, and the people's livelihood and economy are even more unbearable to ask. The national economy also bears its disadvantages, especially with our industry and commerce,"

"The future development of all industries has a close relationship and a huge impact. Merchants live here, and their knowledge is deeper. They dare not block it from above, and they are by no means merely seeking private interests. The lightness and heaviness of the tax rate are linked to the fullness and emptiness of prices. The cost increases, and the selling price also increases. Therefore, although the harm to merchants is obvious, the loss is still shallow. The pain to the people is great, and the concern is even deeper. Now, I heard that there will be a revision of the tax regulations in January next year. For this reason, I have selected several types of iron goods with the most important imbalances in taxation, and narrated the actual situation in detail. I hereby request that the Ministry of Finance approve the transfer of customs tax regulations 187, 207, and 208, the tax rates of scrap iron, waste iron, old iron, and other agricultural and industrial building necessities, be reduced first, and according to the actual value,"

"Taxed at 10 percent to benefit the people's livelihood and relieve business difficulties," etc., have arrived at the meeting. According to the current import tax regulations, there are 16 items of steel taxed ad valorem, among which only 181 railway turnouts and turntables are taxed at 5 percent, and the remaining 7 items are taxed at 15 percent, and the rest are taxed at 10 percent. It is reasonable to present this document and request that your department review and approve the ratio of 10 percent and amend it one by one to benefit the people's livelihood. This is the public's convenience. This is respectfully presented to the Ministry of Finance.
